preached personallie galatia asia whether ye also bithynia doe certeinly know furthermost two certain preache straugers thei call forreiners namely come fro place borne countrie wherein wee apostle calleth thei gentile neither thought straunge peter beeyng apostle iewes neuerthelesse write also vnto gentile iewes call proselites admitted state iewes beeyng lineallie stocke blood abraham notwithstandyng embraced iudaisme submitted theim selues obseruation lawe therefore apostle writeth gentile therefore member common wealthe israell beeyng conuerted faithe adioyned selues faithfull iewes wherefore calleth straungers elect vndoubtedly hee none otherwise reputeth true christian alone writeth whiche maner callyng theim containeth common doctrine wee shall hereafter large heare accordyng foreknowledge god father calleth elect surely selues accordyng ordinance god lieth owne power bryng selues vnto heauen haue faithe wee liste neither god receiue heauen euer naie hee verie diligently circumspectly sifte examine trie awaie therefore mannes doctrine free strength selues thing dependeth god good election vnto sanctification spirite god hath predestinate v holie spirituallie woordes holie spirituall belligods romishe cleargie haue shameleslie taken true professor gospell entailed vnto maumetishe monkerie whiche state thei doe call holie spirituall euen thei monke freere nunne bee shauelyng weare coule peltyng religious habite word spirit signifieth holie hart inwardly spirite god saied especially cause shewe nothing holie whiche god maketh holie v tyme holinesse holinesse whiche sincere altogether entire suche outwarde holinesse iewes nothyng esteemed regarded god sort doeth scripture call v holie sainctes wee beleeue beeyng yet liuyng earth rabbines papistes haue taken name v saiyng holie thei onely holie whiche heauen must therefore repossesse againe take notable name vnto v thou must needes holie yet must thou thinke thou haste holinesse thy self thine owne merite thou art therefore holie thou haste worde god kyngdome heauen thine thou art become entirely righteous holy christ thinges must thou confesse thou wilte bee christian extreme ignominie blasphemie name christ denie honour blood beleeue onely synnes cleane washed awaie wee sanctified thou must beleeue therefore confesse thou art holie yet blood christe thine owne righteousnesse thou must doe suche certaintie constancie cause thou maiest sticke neede spende euen thy life boldly abide looke whatsoeuer maie herevpon come vnto thee obedience sprincklyng blood iesus christe sorte saieth apostle commeth passe wee bee holie wee beleeue obey woorde christ sprinckled blood sainct peter hath vsed somewhat maner speeche sainct paule yet effecte muche paule saieth wee saued faithe christe faithe whiche maketh wee bee attentiue obediente christ holie worde wherefore obey word god muche bee subiect christ bee sprinckled blood beleeue verie greeuous nature bee wholie subiecte christe altogether forslowe ceasse owne matter altogether neglect owne cause counte doe synnes nature therefore stoutly resisteth striueth againste doctrine yet neuerthelesse must laste stoupe yeeld self thereunto sprincklyng read psalme sprinckle hysop lorde shalbe cleane alludeth lawe moses whence saincte peter tooke kinde speeche thereby reuele moses vnto v bryng v kynges highwaie rightly vnderstandyng scripture whe moses builded tabernacle tooke blood goates therewith sprinckled bothe tabernacle people sprincklyng inwardlie sanctifie spirite onely outwardlie externall thinges therefore neede spirituall clensyng forasmuche sanctification outward carnall whereof regarde god yet god thereby type figure signifie spirituall sanctification whiche peter saieth thus muche effecte iewes please selues outwarde holinesse wherby thei thought righteous good life men thei counte emong reprobate howbeit haue sprincklyng farre better ye sprinckled spirite clensed inwardlie iewes sprinckle selues blood goates outwardlie ye sprinckled conscience inwardly harte cleane therefore herein haue greate cause reioyce hereof gentile bee gentile euen righteous iewes righteous sprincklyng thynges chaunged altered none sprinklyng required whiche maie conuert v make v spirituall sprinkle sort nothyng el preache christe hath cause shed blood onely make intercession v vnto father saie moste deare father thou seest blood whiche haue shedde synner thou doe beleeue thou art truelie sprinkled thus thou seest true maner sprinklyng pope monkes sacrificyng priestes iumble true faithe whiche turkes iewes haue saie beleeue god maker bothe heauen earth thus doeth deuill also beleeue yet doeth beleefe nothyng profite hym thei presume come sight god without christe mediator thus saieth sainct paule fift romanes wee haue accesse vnto god faithe selues christ wherefore wee must haue christe v wee must come hym wee must satisfie god hym doe thinges god hym name effect whiche sainct peter saieth place asmuche saied certeinly looke eternall life although wee liue earth yet otherwise resurrection christe saie euen therefore risen againe ascended heauen sitteth right hande father cause hee ascende might giue vnto v spirit whereby beyng regenerate might bee bolde goe father saie behold come thee mercifull father praie vnto thee putte trust confidence praier myne owne lorde christ doeth make intercession myne aduocate wordes carie ardent efficacie fierie force harte beleeueth harte beleeueth suche word colde neither doeth conscience feele comfort thereby wee maie also iudge knowe whiche syncere doctrine true christian preaching hee preacher gospell must moste zelously diligently preache forthe resurrection christ whiche doeth apostle summe faithe bookes best excellentest whiche teache treate vpon poincte principally chiefly hath beene declared article faith waightie importaunce christ risen againe comforte hope vaine whatsoeuer christ hath either done suffred v steede therefore maner teaching moste requisite beholde christ hath dyed v taken vpon satisfie v iustice father sinne death hell moste sharpe bitter encountrie yet could none ouercome hym hym conquered subdued stronger rose mawgre force brought subiection none cause set v free libertie daunger thraldome wee stedfastlie beleeue wee haue perfect assuraunce full possession benefites whiche beyng eche waie impossible bee brought passe selues strength v behoued christ performe otherwise cause haue descended heauen hither among v vile wretched sinfull men therefore men preachyng attribute thinges woorkes thei doe nothyng el cause necessarie pointes doctrine cannot afterwards take place harte hearer rightly vnderstood well ought thinges knowen v christian throughly ought epistle vnderstoode v inheritaunce immortall vndefiled fadeth awaie wee hope suche substaunce inheritaunce present wee liue hope inheritaunce whiche present deede immortall also vndefiled fadeth awaie inheritaunce wee haue perpetually without ende howbeit wee doe yet ee wordes forcible wonderfull efficacie whose minde thei firmely fixed thinke little mooued desire rich pleasure worlde bee one set minde vpon transitorie rich delightes beleeue thynges whiche bee spoken worldlie wealthe terrene treasure bee compared thinges appeareth straight thinges worlde endure small tyme doe sone passe awaie thinges continue euer doe neuer faile fade moreouer thynges worlde vnpure doe defile v man godly one respect caried away defiled vanity pleasaunt thinges life inheritaunce vndefiled pure possesseth remaineth euer immaculate finally inheritance doeth fade doeth decaie neither euer subiect corruption euery yearthly thyng although bee hard iron stone neuerthelesse chaunged continueth still soone man also becommeth old beautie gone becommeth lothsome vnamiable howbeit inheritance farre mutation chaunge alwaies remaineth alwaies freshe floorishyng pleasure greate yearth whiche continuance become lothsome tedious see laste tediousnesse thynges good thynges spoken otherwise whereof sacietie euer whiche obtaine christ mercie god firmely beleeue thei freely giuen vnto v miserable men owne workes merite greate good thynges whiche reason vnderstandyng man able muche comprehende imagination harte conceiue reserued heauen inheritaunce immortall vndefiled fadeth awaie vndoubtedly onely little remoued kepte sight vntill eye bee closed vpp mortall life ended shall certainly finde see vnlesse wee bee vnbeleeuyng wee doubte certaintie thereof apostle addeth inheritaunce whereunto corruption cleaue reserued v heauen whiche kepte power god faithe vnto saluation hope saieth apostle looke excellent inheritance whereunto wee come faithe doe sorte followe one woorde wrought v faithe faithe newe birth newe birthe wee come vnto hope wee certainly looke thynges throughlie assured thereof wherefore sainct peter fitly saieth thynges must doen faithe workes apostle expressely saieth ye power god kepte vnto saluation many hauyng heard gospell faithe onely doeth iustifie without woorkes doe burst forthe saie wee also doe beleeue thinkyng bare opinion whiche thei feine vnto theim selues right faithe wee haue alreadie taught scripture power dooe euen least good woorke without especiall assistaunce god spirite shall wee owne strength arrogate whiche moste excellent namely beleeue cogitation therefore mere dreame thinges vaine fonde god power must bee present woorke v sainct paule writeth ephes god giue vnto spirite wisedome yee maie knowe exceadyng greatnesse power v warde whiche beleeue accordyng woorkyng mightie power c onely god also certaine power doe beleue wherby wee learne lesse matter make faithe one create againe heauen earth wee maie euidently perceiue therefore thei little knowe thei saie whiche vse suche woordes onely faithe doe seeyng many beleeue whiche doe good woorkes thei thinke owne imagination bee faithe faithe also maie bee without good woorkes wee saie saincte peter faithe power god soeuer god woorketh thus regenerate new borne creature faith naturally followe good woorkes wherefore shalbe needelesse saie christia doe doe good woorke forasmuche owne accorde vnbidden worketh nothyng good woorkes howbeit bee hereof admonished dooe deceiue hym self false counterfaite supposed faithe doe therefore take regarde vaine talker prattle muche thynges whose woordes notwithstandyng winde e trifle paule speaketh cor come vnto knowe wordes puffed vp spirituall power kyngdome god consisteth woordes power power god neither true faithe good woorkes wherefore thei vndoubtedly liers whiche boaste themselues name faith christ doe notwithstanding leade leude wicked life assuredly power god bee present thei become maner men suche meaneth whereas peter saith power god ye kepte vnto saluation surely euen faithe whiche power god beeyng v wherewith wee replenished doeth woorke v thing noble excellente wee haue certaine manifeste knowledge thynges pertaine saluation beeyng able iudge freely pronounce thinges whiche yearth example doctrine sincere sounde corrupt false life good euill well dooen otherwise soeuer suche man doeth define determine deede hee bee deceiued preserued kepte power god remaineth iudge doctrine contrariwise faithe power god nothyng error blindnesse reason caried away hither thither one woorke asmuche striueth owne woorkes come vnto heauen therefore alwaies thinketh behold bryng heauen let worke shall bee partaker eternall felicitie blessednesse hereupon haue ouerspread worlde suche rabble swarmes monastery altar sacrificyng priestes monkes frier votary suche greate blindnesse doth god suffer fall whiche doe beleeue v beleeue hee preserueth affordeth right vnderstandyng thynges wee maie bee condemned blindnesse mercie attaine saluation prepared shewed laste tyme inheritaunce whereunto ye appoincted alreadie purchased beginnyng worlde prepared hid yet couered closed sealed vp shall moment opened reueiled maie plainly see wherein ye reioyce though season neede require ye heauinesse manifolde tentations thou bee christian lookest inheritaunce saluation thou must needes wholy depende vppon vtterly conteinne earthly thynges thou must also confesse openly affirme vnderstandyng wisedome holinesse worlde altogether nothing wherfore thou must looke worlde condemne persecute thee therefore hath sainct peter rightlie ioyned together three faithe hope crosse affliction asmuche one proceedeth howbeit giueth small comfort suffer persecution woordes dooe sounde thus heauinesse shall endure little afterward ye shall euer reioyce saluation alreadie prepared wherfore bee meane season pacient affliction whiche ye suffer right christian consolation doctrine men doe comfort whiche haue relation bee ridde deliuered outward discommodities apostle speaketh suche corporall comfort discommoditie outward trouble come good courage sustaine suffer ye thinke ye maie shake theim bee deliuerd theim rather thinke thus selues mine inheritance alreadie prepared affliction shall shortly cease shall temporall comfort bee taken awaie eternall consolation whiche wee haue god supplie place thereof moreouer word diligently noted whiche apostle addeth saieth neede require whiche effect vttereth also afterward chapter woordes god bee many men certaine force striue come vnto heauen euen chruste therefore laye vpon selues crosse affliction accordyng owne opinion iudgement fondlie reason giuen extoll owne woorkes god vtterlie disalloweth suche dealyng owne woorkes whiche wee make choise force hym must looke laie vppon v sende vnto v maie walke followe whither doeth lead guide v wherefore neede thou shouldest seeke procure thy self affliction neede require bee god thou shalte suffer chearefullie take crosse vppon thee comforte thy self hope expectation saluation whiche temporall eternall triall faith much precious golde perisheth though tried fire might founde c effect crosse manifolde affictions whiche wee suffer life syncere faith maie bee knowne whiche false counterfait cause doeth lord afflict v faith maie tried exercysed made manifest world others also maie bee inuited wonne faithe example wee last maie attaine vnto glorie wee praise god againe also praise glorifie honour v counterfait liyng hipocrites haue contemned right waie shall subiect shame confusion scripture doeth often compare crosse vnto fire sainct peter compareth gold tried fire triall faith whiche made crosse affliction fire doeth diminishe golde clenseth purifieth whatsoeuer drossie substaunce mixed maie separated sorte layeth god crosse vpon christian whereby thei maie scoured polished well saied apostle trial faith c faith must tried purified euen worde pure whereunto alone ye must sticke trust vnto nothyng el purgyng scouryng polishyng v crosse daily necessary v otherwise olde dull adam would still muche hang vppon v dull spirite make faith vnpure suche life true christian continually becometh better purer worde gospell wee doe beleeue wee iustified beginne purged yet long fleshe altogither cleane pure therefore doeth god cast v middest fire affliction ignominie trouble whereby wee daily purged vntill suche tyme wee dye purgyng wee attaine vnto workes owne outwarde worke purifie harte within faith sorte tried whatsoeuer mixed feined counterfait must needes bee remoued separated hereupon last christe shall appeare shall followe magnificent honour praise glorie reioyce ioye vnspeakeable glorious receiuyng ende faith euen saluation soules apostle saieth haue vnspeakeable glorious gladnesse ioye bringeth honour glorie worlde hath suche ioye whereof cometh ignominie shame sainct peter speaketh true spirituall ioye plainly thou shalt reade almost whole scripture yet could fully vtter declare thing haue bin saied part preface wherein apostle sheweth faith christ also must proued purged aduersities affliction whiche god doth sende followeth faith contained promised scripture whiche saluation prophet haue inquired searched whiche prophesied grace come vnto searchyng tyme spirite whiche testified christe whiche declare suffrynges come vnto christ glorie followe vnto reueiled vnto selues vnto v minister thinges whiche shewed vnto whiche haue preached vnto gospell holy ghost sent downe fro heauen thinges angel desire beholde sainct peter diligent learnyng scripture whereby wee maie bee certein throughly confirmed faith sorte doeth sainct paule also call v scripture first chapter romanes saieth god promised gospel afore prophet holy scripture also saieth rom faith whereby wee iustified witnessed lawe prophet reade also act preached faith thessalonica called scripture expounded vnto also side searched scripture daily whether thynges sainct paule teach behoueth v doe also thynges whiche reade newe testament wee maie learne confirme olde wherein wee shall see promise concernyng christ whereof christ also hath admonished v iohn searche saieth scripture beare witnesse mee againe ye beleeue moses ye would also beleeue wrote mee vaine ianglers therefore bee regarded whiche contemne olde testament presumptuously saie wee haue neede thereof notwithstandyng alone must taken foundation grounde faith ende god sent prophet iewes thei might testifie vnto christe come wherefore apostle euery conuince refell iewes owne scripture prouyng iesus christ cause bookes moses prophet gospel forasmuche reade thinges foretolde concernyng christe whiche afterwarde beyng doeu accomplished apostle preache write difference onely whereas bookes bothe committed writing yet withstanding much requisite gospel new testament contained writyng preached voyce whiche maie openly publishe sounde forth maie heard euery worlde whereas also written necessary whereas olde testament doeth speake onely christ come gospel liuely word vocall preachyng christe alreadie come betweene bookes olde testament moreouer difference first fiue bookes moses summe whole scripture peculiarly called olde testament history also bookes wherein described deedes diuers example whiche obserued moses lawe also transgressed lastly prophet whiche haue plaine relation writyngs moses haue largely plainer wordes expressed howbeit one meaning moses al prophetes whereas wont saied olde testament abrogated reiected thus bee vnderstoode first difference betweene olde newe testament wee haue saied olde signifieth christe come newe doeth performe exhibite present thynges old promised figure shadowed forth signified wherfore type figure doe cease forasmuche accomplished performed whiche thei signifie fulfilled thei promise neither ought bee obserued hereafter choyce meates apparell place tymes thei christe thei referred made indifferent vse obseruaunces saue iewes neither giuen ende thei thereby bee iustified thei set forth christ come furthermore old testament god double rule gouermente one inward outward gouerned people bothe inwardly harte outwardly bodie externall affaire therefore giue vnto theim many lawes mingled one househande might giue bill diuorcement wife would keepe put awaie hym pertained outward rule regiment belonged spirituall gouerment whereas god commaunded theim loue neighbour themselues howbeit ruleth onely spiritually ouer v christ corporally outwardly ciuill magistrate wherefore christe come externall outward gouernment taken awaie doeth commaunde v putte difference betweene outward persones tymes place doeth gouerne v spiritually woorde wee lordes thynges without v bounde tyed corporall thynges thynges whiche pertaine spirituall administration gouernment taken awaie still force thynges whiche thou readest moses concernyng loue god thy neighbour god haue duely obserued lawe condemne doe beleue figure also haue place sense spiritually thei spirituall thynges signified outwarde figure whiche outward thynges taken awaie housebande refuse wife adultery sake put awaie hym whiche figure certaine spirituall signification whiche afterward spiritually fulfilled god sorte refuse obstinate iewes whiche would beleeue christe chose gentile whiche dooeth euen yet also prouidyng refuseth liue faithe bee caste churche christ maie repente sorte constitution also wherein ordeined woman bee maried brother housebande beyng deade bryng forthe child hym must bee called name hym deade possesse substaunce albeeit bee abolished yet neuerthelesse figure whiche signifieth somethyng concernyng christe brother hath died v ascention heauen commauded v gospel make soules spouse pregnant fruitefull hereuppon wee retaine name named hym whose moste excellent rich succeede yet must boaste saie haue conuerted wonne men suche effectes must onely attributed vnto christ maie saied also figure old testament whiche long tedious seuerally rehearse whatsoeuer olde testament externall outwarde yet force efficacie saiynges prophetes concernyng faithe loue whiche christ confirmeth matth saieth whatsoeuer ye would menne doe euen doe ye hem lawe prophet moreouer moses prophetes witness christ beyng come tyme preache christ onely sauiour shall doe conueniently takyng place chapter genesis namely thy seede shall nation yearth bee blessed dooe therevppon liuely voice inferre christe seede abraham men must bee blessed hereof followeth adam cursed damnable therefore necessarie wee desire bee deliuered damnation beleeue seede vpon suche seiynges wee muste grounde faithe wherefore wee ought duely regard reuerentlie esteeme theim muche thei testifie beare witnesse christ faithe maie bee established confirmed whiche peter doeth woordes followyng whiche saluation prophetes haue enquited searched whiche prophesied grace come vnto sort sainct paule also speaketh last chapter epistle romanes reuelation mysterie whiche kept secret since worlde beganne opened published among nation scripture prophetes many saiynges thou maiest read newe testament taken prophetes whereby apostle haue proued thynges dooen accomplished thet foretolde prophetes christe matth rehearseth saiyng esaie blinde see halt goe c none otherwise would saie thing ye read written ye see truely dooen verie deede performed read also sainct paule actes apolios act thei couinced iewes preued scripture iesus christe whatsoeuer prophetes foretolde accomplished fulfilled euill actes apostle sorte shewe gospell must preached gentile thei also might bee brought faithe bee assured thinges therefore dooen common endeuour iewes might conuinced compelled acknowledge thynges dooen thei reade foretolde scripture searchyng tyme spirite whiche testified christe whiche theim declare sufferynges come vnto christ meanyng sainct peter albeit prophetes plainly knowe certaine definite tyme yet generally thei signifie circumstance bothe tyme place christe suffer death dye gentile beleeue hym signes whiche thei foretold might bee certainly knowne time come prophet daniel came verie nere matter neuerthelesse spake thereof obscurely darckly namely tyme christ suffer dye thing come passe thei undoubted prophecie kyngdome iewes ceasse christe come daie certaine tyme bee fulfilled expressed forasmuche sufficiente knowe tyme come commyng christe farre ioel second chapter prophecie fore shewed time holie ghost come last day powre spirite vppon fleshe whiche prophecie sainct peter seconde chapter actes rehearseth thereby proueth foretold tyme brother whiche liued hereby thou seest diligence alwaies apostle rendered reason thynges whiche thei preached taught approuing scripture cou cels pope would doe thynges v without scripture comaundyng v obedience churche vnder paine excommunication beleue apostle replenished holie ghoste certaine bothe thei sent christ also thei preache true vndoubted gospell yet thei humble submit selues thus farre thei required beleeued nothyng whiche thei proue soundlie scripture bee thei affirmed mouthes infidel might stopped able saie nothyng reason shall wee beleeue grosse vnlearned lubber whiche neither preache woorde god neither doe thyng iangle prate bauie reuile could yt father thus erre long since concluded wherefore thinges ought reason giuen man wee able proue certainly scripture none shalbee saued beleeueth christe men able speake thyng againste also thei shall neuer bee able proue vnto v childishe trifle scripture namely damnable ease whiche fasteth daie suche like wherefore meete neither ought wee hande beleeue sainete peter saieth moreouer glorie followe whiche spoken apostle maie bee vnderstoode bothe affliction whiche christ self suffered also wee christian member doe suffer sainct paule calleth sufferyng christe whiche euery christian doeth suffer affiance name worde woorkes christe myne forasmuche firmely beleeue affliction also asmuche afflicted sake wherefore affliction christ daily accomplished christian euen vnto ende worlde small comfort vnto v howsoeuer thinges fall wee certaine affliction common togither christe v counteth otherwise owne also maie little encrease comforte glorie shall vndoubtedly followe affliction howbeit wee must knowe also christ came vnto glorie hee suffered wee also must first beare crosse hym maie afterwardes reioyce togither thinges therefore saieth apostle effect whiche wee dode preache prophetes haue long since manifestly declared foretolde thei come passe holie ghoste reuellyng vnto whereas wee doe little vnderstande prophetes cause wee ignorant tongue wherin thei write thei haue written plainly manifestly wherefore skilfull tongue haue spirite god whiche vndoubtedly beleeue haue harde vnderstande muche thei know unto whole scripture tendeth bothe tongue vnderstood spirite wantyng appeareth otherwise prophetes madde dronken howbeit wee want either farre better haue spirite without tongue tongue without spirit prophetes spake sorte apostle yet signifie thinges afterward apostle preached bothe shewe many thinges affliction aswell christe beleeue also glorie followeth dauid psal hee speaketh christ sorte wo e man doth el declare exceeding debasing whiche passion hee suffered also psal writeth affliction christian sayng wee counted sheepe appoincted slaine c vnto also reueiled vnto selues vnto v minister thynges whiche shewed vnto whiche haue preached vnto gospell holy ghoste sent downe heauen sufficient prophetes knewe thynges left behinde writyng sake makyng themselues herein minister vnderstandyng hereof wee might learne maisters thus haue wee sure helpe strengthenyng faithe better instruction whereby wee maie bee able defende selues false doctrine whiche thinges angel desire beholde greate thinges haue apostle delared vnto v holy ghoste whiche came downe vppon heauen euen angel doe desire beholde see wee muste greate attention shut eye see gospell wherein surely haue exceedyng delight ioye consolation yet see thynges bodily eye wee must beleeue wee made partaker righteousnesse truth saluation good thinges god hath inasmuche hath giuen vnto v christe onely begotten sonne fountaine head good thinges hee hym giue v also good thynges rich treasure whereat angel heauen doe take merueilous ioye delight thynges offered vnto v gospell beleeue must needes likewise take merueilous delight pleasure therein howbeit delight pleasure wee liue earth ca perfect angel beginneth v faith wee haue certein feelyng thereof heauen shall bee greate harte man able comprehende yet shall enioye come thither thus thou seest saincte peter teacheth v arme prepare selues scripture hitherto hath described preache gospell foretolde prophetes bee sorte preached taught hee proceedeth hereafter exhorteth v faithe embrace loue followe suche preachyng gospell saiyng wherfore girde vp loynes mind bee sober trust perfectly grace brought vnto reuelatio iesus christ obedient child fashioning selues vnto former lustes ignorance whiche hath called holy ye holy maner conuersation written bee ye holy holy exhortation faith meaning wherof forasmuche greate thynges preached giuen vnto gospell whiche euen angel doe desire pleasure beholde see ye faithfully cleaue vnto assured trust affiance repose hope therein faithe maie bee sincere sounde fained opinion dreame girde vp loynes mynde sainct peter speaketh spirituall girdyng mynde like man corporally girde sworde vppon loynes girdyng christ maketh mention luke saieth let loynes girded place scripture loynes signifie carnall lust concupiscence sainct peter speaketh spirituall loynes whereas scripture speaketh bodie calleth part loynes whence father proceedeth naturall generation according read gen christ spring loynes iuda wherefore corporally girde loynes signifieth nothing el chastitie esay chap righteousnesse shall girdle loynes faithfulnesse girdle reynes onely faithe filthie vnlawfull lust restrained brideled spirituall girdyng whereof apostle speaketh sorte virgin bodie chast entire mynde faithe whereby espoused christ spiritually sounde sincere howbeit sone reuolteth faithe false erroneous doctrine violate corrupted wherevppon scripture commonly calleth infidelitie idolatrie name adulterie fornication namely mynde sticketh doctrine forsaketh faithe christ sainct peter dehorteth hee biddeth girde vp loynes mynde effect asmuche saie ye haue heard gospell attained vnto faithe see ye persist therein suffer selues defiled corrupted false doctrine waueryng vncertentie waie waie apostle sainct peter vseth certen peculiar proper kinde speeche suche sainct paule vseth saith gird vp loynes mynde hee calleth mynde otherwise call thought saie thinke thus right sainct paule saieth dooe wee thinke suche opinion seemes vnto v meanes doeth apostle moste properly signifie faith meanyng thus much effect ye haue attained true thought setled right perswasion wee iustified faithe onely persist strongly herein girde fast vnto valiauntly sticke thereunto let man pull sounde opinion harte shall yee prosperously persener stande many false teacher arise forge doctrine men thereby corrupte mynde looze girdle faithe wherefore harte receiue admonition whiche giue aforehande doctrine truthe maie well fixed mynde maie valiauntly persiste therein hypocrite whiche truste woorkes liue honest vertuous life appeareth outwardly dooe verily thinke fully perswaded god muste needes receiue theim heauen woorkes maketh proude presumptuous glorious owne conceiptes pharisey mentioned luke whereof also marie maketh mention song commonly called magnificat vseth woorde whiche thou readest sainct peter hath scattered proude imagination harte hath ouerthrowne brought confusion deuises owne myndes thoughtes bee sober sobrietie perteineth outwardly bodie especiall woorke faithe although manne bee iustified yet free euill desire deede faithe hath begonne restraine bridle fleshe notwithstandyng doeth continually striue assaulteth sondrie sortes desire whiche goe aboute accordyng concupiscence thereof againe burst forthe preuaile wherefore spirite hath daiely muche adoe bridle restraine must therefore without intermission haue continuall fight alwaies take greate heede fleshe least tyme suche craftinesse thereof vndermine supplant faithe premiss appeareth farre thei deceiue theim selues whiche boste thei haue faithe coumpt sufficient liuyng meane season according owne lustes desire true faithe muste needes bee earnest endeuour keepe bodie vnder holde bridle outragyng doyng listeth herevpon sainct peter exhorteth v bee sober howbeit biddeth v destroye bodie weaken meete haue doen whiche haue made selues mad ouer muche fastyng yea haue quite pined consumed themselues waie fonde error tyme sainct bernard although otherwise holy man afflicted bodie great abstinence reason noysome breathe whiche hee gott thereby man could abide stande neere hym bee companie hee length deliuered error willed brother thei much pine pinche body well sawe vndue abstinence made vnfit serue brother wherefore sainct peter requireth wee sober wee doe muche farre restraine fleshe wee feele wantonnesse vnrulinesse thereof require hee appointeth certen tyme pope hath doen long wee must faste leaueth euery one iudgement fast hee bee alwaies sober hee doe surcharge bodie ouermuche eatyng drinking maie haue perfect vse reason knowe vse sens aright liue profitably beneficially others vocation preposterous absurde vnprofitable thyng giue generall precept hereof vnto whole people churche asmuche wee vnlike among selues one hath strong bodie another weake needefull one absteine muche absteine little bodie maie neuerthelesse remaine health bee fit doe good workes againe bee deale cleane contrarily thinke thei doe well fastyng nothyng supposyng thei maie without respecte tyme eate thei herein thei doe well albeit thei haue somewhat tasted gospell yet haue thei profited little nothyng like vnto former thei haue profited onely contemne lawes pope thei girde vp mynde sens peter biddeth neither thei bridle desire bodie sluggishnesse lasciuiousnesse thereof maie bee repressed good faste howbeit right faste deede giue bodie nourishmente needefull preserue healthe also exercise labour watchynges least old asse become wanton lasciuious meete let hym bee restrained bridled obedient spirite whiche saincte peter calleth bee sober wont faste excessiuely engorge pamper selues fishe beste sortes wine one diner thei make beallies like taber drumme stuffyng crammyng full truste perfectly grace brought vnto svche christian faithe affiaunce wholie trusteth woorde god quietly committeth self vnto confidently attempteth whatsoeuer teacheth whereupon peter saith loynes mynde girded vp faith sincere sounde ye doe quietly confidently commit selues worde god bolde vpon trust therein hauyng regarde whatsoeuer thyng commeth perill whether bee rich good name bodie euen life self excellently therefore hath wordes described sincere vnfeined faithe faithe must sluggishe sleepie whiche rather dreame faithe must bee liuely effectuall one would confidence offer self affliction trouble whatsoeuer depende wholy woorde esteemyng indifferently whatsoeuer state god sendeth wee maie patiently susteine aduersitie well enioye prosperitie example sake must dye must confidently commit self christe muste quietly offer life sake trustyng woorde whiche deceiue muste boldly couragiously triumpht ouer myne aduersaries needfull moreouer faith passe without declinyng waie suffer self hindered terrified meanes remoue fro eye whatsoeuer seeth heareth feeleth suche faithe doeth sainct peter require whiche consisteth thinkyng woordes mightie power effectuall vertue saieth sainct peter trust perfectlie grace brought vnto saie haue deserued exceadyng greate grace euen freelie offered brought vnto gospell whiche declareth publisheth grace vnto v wee selues haue neither deuised found holie ghost hath sent fro heauen worlde thyng brought vnto v forsooth euen thinges whiche wee haue afore mentioned namelie whosoeuer beleeueth christe cleaueth faste vnto woorde hath together hym benefites blessynges whiche bee muche thereby euen lorde ouer synne death deuill helle moste certainly assured euerlastyng life greate treasure brought home v owne doores laied vp bosomes without owne helpe merite deseruyng yea euen vnhoped vnlooked neither knewe muche thought suche matter therefore apostle exhorteth v wee boldlie vndoubtedlie looke grace god whiche offereth bestoweth vpon v wise lye reuelation iesu christe god offereth grace none christ therefore without mediatour lette presume come sight haue afore admonished heare manne hym bryngeth hym christe moste deare sonne bee aduocate spokesman one onely hath respecte vnto sake faithe cleaue faste vnto hym therefore requireth handes acknowledge sonne persone whose blood wee one hym dare present selues hym ende came lord christ taking flesh blood vnto ioyned hymself v hee might obtaine pardon purchase grace v yt hades father faith christ prophetes patriarch saued behooued menne generally beleeue promise made vnto abraham thy seede shall nation bee blessed therefore iewes turkes thei repose truste owne workes hopyng thereby winne heauen haue faithe therefore dooeth peter saie grace brought yet reuelation iesu christe speake plainly iesus christe reuealed vnto gospell shewed vnto v christe maie throughly knowe hym namely sauiour taketh awaie sinnes deliuereth v misery reconcileth v vnto father without workes doeth iustifie saue v soeuer doeth thus acknowledge christ altogether deceiued albeit thou knowe hym bee sonne god died rose againe sitteth right hande father yet hast thou thereby throughly knowne christ neither shall knowyng hym whitt auaile thee vnlesse thou proceede steppe bothe knowe also beleeue thynges thee helpe relieue comfort thee vaine therefore al thynges whiche hitherto haue obtruded preached vnto v schoolemen insomuche thei without knowledge christ entred commonly consideration thereof onely thinke muche sorrowe greef lorde christ sustained passion though sitteth idle heauen takyng care v ioiyng hym self whereby people harte remaine vtterly drie without right vse heauenly dew water soules liuely faithe growe take roote christe ought thus bee preached liueth raigneth hym self wise neede hym descende worlde shedde precious blood sith sent worlde hym worlde might bee saued hymself third ihon declareth needefull accomplishe performe selfsame thyng whiche sent father woorde sent commyng vnderstoode diuine nature christe onely rather humaine nature office whiche bore executed immediately baptized beganne deale office doe wherevnto sent whiche came worlde namely shewe declare truthe vnto menne many beleeued hym bee saued sorte therefore hee openly published hymself woorkyng meanes might knowne offring grace owne self vnto v obedient child behaue selues becommeth obedient child obedience scripture signifieth faithe pope doctorlie schoolemen cloistered diuines hath gloses mangled woorde wrested maintenaunce lye trifle thei haue dooen whatsoeuer el reade scripture concernyng obedience namely notable saiyng reg obedience better sacrifice thei sawe highlie obedience commended scripture thei haled forced proper vnto theim selues thereby blinde worlde bryng menne errour thinke obedience greatly commended scripture nothyng el embrace allowe soeuer thei enioyne laie vppon theim meanes doe thei drawe v woorde god liyng legendaries deuelishe obedience whereas deede obedient child god heareth gospell woorde god faithe embraceth therefore whatsoeuer woorde giue eare vnto rather stampe tread vnder thy feete fashionyng selues vnto former lustes ignoraunce bee maners neither haue suche conuersation aforetyme haue let man see life whiche heretofore haue ledde liued heretofore idolater liued luste surphette drunkennesse couetousnesse pride wrathe enuie hatred whiche euill heathennishe life yea rather mere infidelitie desperate forlorne conuersation walked blinde ignoraunt wottyng therefore put ye awaie euil desire thou seest imputeth mischeeues vnto ignoraunce vnto spring thei procede flowe perfect faithe true knowledge christ lackyng nothing el errour blindnesse menne liue vtterly ignoraunt right wrong thereby runne headlong without stoppe staie mischeeues inconueniences sort hitherto haue wee dealt withall christe darkened almoste abolished banished worlde steede truthe wee nozzeled errour place sincere knowledge truth wee fast chained clogged ignorance muche within question mooued debated worlde ouer meanes wee might attaine felicitie infallible signe blindnesse ignoraunce sincere knowledge faithe extinct taken awaie herevpon grewe worlde pestered suche number sectes thynges torne sonder disordered euery manne framed owne imagination peculier seuerall waie hymself heauen euill sith wee able waie helpe selues wee choose alwaies bee drowned deeper deeper gapyng gulphe vtter blindenesse therefore sainct peter woordes saie haue long inough walked foolishnesse caste awaie beeyng wise hauyng raught vnto true knowledge whiche hath called holie euen bee ye holie maner conuersation witten bee ye holie holie doeth sainct peter alledge place old testament leuitie lorde saieth bee ye holie holie saie lorde god people meete bee rightly throughly plaieth parte lorde deede bendeth care make people like vnto hymself dutifully eche respect behaue selues towardes hym frame theim selues seruiceable herevpon falleth lorde god holie also people bee holie walke faithe verie little mention made scripture sainctes holie men departed life alwaies maner speaketh holie menne yet aliue prophet dauid pronounceth holie psalme saiyng preserue thou soule lorde holie smatteryng doctorlie diuines schoolemen haue also misconstrued peruerted true sense place saiyng prophete hath peculier reuelation calleth holie wherein thei flatly bewraie themselues bothe lacke faithe also vtterly vnacquainted reuelation christ thei thei might easely effect feele selues power therof christian hath feelyng suche reuelation conscience hath feelyng christia christian commeth communion christ partaker goodnesse therfore seyng christ holie member must also needes holie el deny christe holie thou bee baptized thou haste put garment holinesse whiche christe sainct paule testifieth worde holie signifieth whiche onely proper vnto god hym onely doeth appertaine commonly doe call consecrated therefore doth sainct peter saie haue consecrated selues vnto god therefore standeth vppon looke ye suffer selues bee caried awaie againe vaine lustes desire worlde giue place vnto god hee maie raigne liue woorke shall ye bee holie euen hee holie thus hath hitherto described grace offered vnto v gospell preachyng christe hath taught v againe ought behaue selues toward namely persist continue pure sincere perswasion faithe well assured worke whatsoeuer either doe deuise thing auaile v toward saluatio doctrine preached straightwaies reason commeth inferreth thus case stande neede haue doe good worke doe grosseheads enter fonde opinion rather mere madnesse makyng right christian life carnall licentiousnesse deemyng lawfull euery man dooe listeth suche maner persones doeth sainct peter place meete withall preuention taketh aforehande foolishe imagination teachyng v christian libertie without dependyng vpon good workes bee vsed towardes god hym onely build faithe without workes hereby wee attribute vnto hym due due honour acknowledge hym good god bothe iust true mercifull suche faithe deliuereth offereth v fro sinnes mischeeues whatsoeuer haue attributed vnto god al residue liues haue liue bestowe benefite neighbor serue doe good vnto hym cheefest principallest worke others proceeding issuyng faith mouthes readie confesse christ bloud also beare witnesse vnto hym case require bestowe liues also sake yet hath god neede worke therefore must wee doe faithe beyng thereby throughly tried manifested maie also drawe allure others like furthermore bee woorkes dooe generallie also serue ende wee maye thereby doe good vnto neighbor whiche notwithstandyng wee selues god hee must worke bryng passe v thus haue wee nothyng worlde owne wee ascribe respecte vnto selues hereby euidently appeareth farre preaching gospell doeth open yea neuer little windowe liue carnallie euery man maie lawfullie doe listeth therefore saieth sainct peter furthermore ye call father whiche without respect persone iudgeth according euery man woorke passe tyme dwellyng feare knowyng yee redeemed corruptible thinges siluer golde vaine conuersation receiued tradition father precious bloud christ lambe vndefiled without spot whiche ordeined foundation worlde declared laste tymes sake whiche meanes dooe beleeue god raised dead gaue glorie faithe hope might god meanyng sainct peter place ye faithe come poinct ye sonnes god father ye haue attained incorruptible inheritaunce whereof hath beene spoken afore therefore remaineth nothing behind veile taken awaie may bee openly shewed earst hidden must ye yet expect looke till tyme come bee giuen see therefore come good poinct maie boldnesse trust inuocate call vppon god father neuerthelesse iust render vnto euery one without respect persones accordyng workes let man perswade hym self dignified entitled worthie name bee called christian sonne god therefore god spare hym hee liue without feare accoumpt enough hee hath suche excellent name worlde deede iudgeth accordyng respectes persones iudgyng persones equallie indifferently spareth suche bee freendes wealthie riche fayre learned wise mightie high authoritie god respecteth none hee dealeth thynges indefferencie bee persones neuer high callyng hee egipt slea childe aswell kyng poorest sheepeheard exod therefore apostle warneth v wee lookyng like iudgement stand feare vasit tytle wee called christian therefore wee presume god whitt spare v hee wil others vaine perswasion long agoe deceiued iewes bragged selues bee seede abraham people god scripture maketh difference accordyng fleshe according spirit true god promised christ borne seede abraham hym come holie people followeth therevpon bee child god whiche descended ligne abraham hee also promised saluation gentile saied hee would saue gentile ariseth question say god doeth saue v onely faithe without respect good workes happeneth sainct peter doeth saie hee iudge accordyng person according euery man worke answere whatsoeuer wee haue taught concernyng faithe alone doeth iustifie v god without al doubt true forasmuch scripture declareth witnesseth plainly bee denyed whereas sainct peter doeth saie god iudgeth accordyng workes also true waie muste vndoubtedly bee beleeued faithe neither good woorke bee againe faithe bee good workes therefore thou muste bryng bothe thy faithe thy good woorkes one bothe together comprehended contained summe true christian life thou liuest therefore shalt thou receiue god iudge thee therfore although god iudge v accordyng woorkes yet neuerthelesse remaineth also alike true good workes onely fruictes faithe whereby shalbe easie finde trie faithe infidelitie therefore god iudge thee accordyng thy workes thereby laie face face thy charge whether thou haue faithe man better confute lyer owne woordes yet neuerthelesse plaine word made lior lyer afore vttered lye lye must needes proceede harte mouth take therefore woordes sainct peter moste simple sense sorte vnderstande workes fruictes seales faithe god doth iudge men according fruictes whiche ensue followe true sounde faithe intent maye manifestly appeare faithe remaineth harte also infidelitie lodgeth god iudge accordyng interrogatory question whether thou called christian whether thou bee baptized hee thus question thee sirrha thou bee christian bee thy fruictes whereby thou art able confirme approue thy faithe therefore saieth sainct peter forasmuche haue suche father iudgeth accordyng man person see yee haue conuersation tyme dwelling feare saie feare ye father feare punishment reuenge wicked reprobate deuilles dooe feare hym feare ye hym least forsake withdrawe holie hande euen honest good childe standeth feare least hee offende father commit thyng bee well liked hym suche feare doeth god require handes whereby wee maye loathe abhorre sinne diligently studie helpe neighbour long haue liue worlde christian beleeueth well possessed goodes benefites god childe god wee haue heard afore declared tyme hee hath liue nothyng el kinde sequestration pilgrimage spirite faithe alreadie heauen whiche hee euen lorde thynges god therefore suffreth hym yet tyme liue fleshe bee conuersant bodie vpon earth purposelie help others bryng heauen therefore wee ought otherwise vse worlde make accompt thereof straungers wayfaring men wont doe commyng lodgyng inne make reckoning haue hostes handes meate drincke lodging one night longer thei doe chalenge laie claime vnto hostes whole substaunce sorte ought euery one accoumpt wealth richesse euen though thei none take therof onely much sufficient maintenance nourishment bodie rest relieue helpe needie neighbour therefore life christian man otherwise mansion one night wee haue permanent dwellyng place wee must haue desire thither father namely heauen therfore wee ought abandon laie aside lasciuiousnesse dissolute life passe sainct peter saieth time dwellyng feare knowyng ye redeemed corruptible thinges siluer golde vaine conuersation receiued tradition father precious bloud christ saieth ought prouoke stirre employe conuersation feare god consideryng greate price redemption coste heretofore ye citezins worlde liuyng vnder tyrannous rule deuill hath god deliuered suche lamentable desperate conuersation hath brought place citezens heauen straungers pilgrim earth marke ye wel muche god hath bestowed vnvaluable exceedyng greate treasure wherewith redeemed brought happie case become child god therefore passe time conuersation feare take ye good heede least ye contemne neglect thynges ye loose excellent precious treasure treasure whiche excellent precious wherewith wee redeemed corruptible thinges golde siluer moste precious bloud christe sonne god treasure excellent price inescimable sense reason man able comprehende insomuche one small droppe innocent bloud fullie sufficient sinnes whole worlde pleased eternall father aboundantly poure grace vpon v suche price procure worke saluation would haue moste deare sonne christ shed bloud bestow giue vnto v treasure therefore requireth v doe cast awaie ayre make small accoumpt suche greate grace rather esteeme wee maie bee stirred mooued vnto feare liuyng therein wee maie deserue est sone depriued surpassing treasure withall must diligently noted considered sainct peter doeth saie ye redeemed vaine conuersation ye receiued tradition father hee vtterlie throweth downe perswasion wee wont moste commonly leane vnto thinkyng dooinges ought bee allowed well liked olde custome haue lon continuaunce auncestours predecessor ng haue many wise good men haue obserued thus hee saieth whatsoeuer father haue either enacted doen ill consequently thinges haue learned theim concernyng worshippe god corrupt naught god muste bestowe blond owne sonne redeeme free men whatsoeuer therefore washed awaie bloud altogether fleshe infected accused wherevpon followeth earnestly man striueth attaine righteousnesse without christ true righteousnesse deeper hee plunged drouned gulphie dungeon blindnesse iniquitie makyng guiltie precious bloud grosse externall vice effect little bee made accoumpt comparison odious sinne teacheth v attaine iustification righteousnesse workes whiche frameth worshipping god according imagination man idle braine phantasie meanes innocent bloud christ dishonored moste shamefully blasphemed euen gentile heathen people farre grieuously sinne honouryng sunne moone whiche thei thought bee true worshipping god thei committyng faultes whiche thei doubt sinfull lewde therefore humane iustification righteousnesse nothyng el mere blasphemie god offence man able commit moste hainous thinges worlde embraceth accoumpteth right worshippe god perfect waie iustification accoumpted greater synne face god faultes whatsoeuer sort professed order religious cloysterers munkes whatsoeuer el hath glorious glitteryng shew iudgement world yet neuerthelesse cleane without faithe therefore whosoeuer bee waie meane seeketh grace god blood better hym neuer come sight god owne beggerlie righteousnesse doeth displease offende diuine maiestie lambe vndefiled without spotte herevpon againe doth sainct peter expounde interprete scripture epistle although breef short wonderfull effectuall pithie riche little afore speaketh vaine conuersation pursuyng tradition father lightly touche sundrie place prophetes namelie place xvj ieremie gentile shall come vnto thee endes worlde shall saie surelie father haue inherited lye vanitie c though saie euen prophetes foretolde redeemed tradition father sorte also leadeth v scripture saieth redeemed precious blood christ lambe vndefiled without spotte dooeth expounde whiche read prophetes moses liij esaie brought sheepe slaughter figure meante xij exod paschall lambe thynges dooeth interprete saieth lambe christe behooued hym bee without blemishe spotte also vndefiled without spotte whose blood shedde v ordeined foundation worlde declared laste tymes wee haue deserued nothyng ne yet muche euer desired thyng precious blood christe bee shedde v therefore cause matter herein whereof wee maie lawfullie selues glorie make bragge glorie apperteineth onely god without ites promised eueiled manifested whiche euerlasting euen fou dation worlde gospell wherefore also last whiche course former tymes expired laste age reueiled vnto v furthermore also accordyng accoumpte computacion tyme ende worlde farre peter seconde epistle third chapter declareth saiyng one daie lorde thousande yeres thousande yeres one daie meanyng thereby call v awaie earnall computation tyme esteeme thereof accordyng iudgemente god wherein certainly laste time finall ende fullie come small tyme lefte behinde remainyng god nothyng saluation reueiled throughlie perfected onely god suffereth worlde thus still stande continue intent might throughlie honored glorified albeit touchyng hymself perfectly reueiled bee looked shalbe perfectlyer manifested sake whiche meanes doe beleeue god raised hym deade gaue hym glorie faithe hope might bee god sake saieth gospell reueiled god christ neede therof doen healthe saluation ende wee beleeue hym neither haue owneselues strength power dooe christe maketh intercession vnto father v raised deade might raigne ouer thynges somuche whiche beleeueth hym hath good thynges bee hym ascendeth vp father meanes haue faithe god faithe also hope onely faithe must saue v yet sure firme faithe god unlesse god helpe thee thou shalt sure euer remaine helplesse therefore purpose though men worlde doe neuer muche fauour thee fauour god onely necessarie wherein thou maiest glorie thy father thou sonne thou reposed greater confidence trust thy rnal father mother thy necessitie bee readie helpe thee euen christes sake onely mediatoure sauiour suche faithe commeth humaine power god planteth th v christe blood deserued merited therefore hath giuen glorie beyng set right hande diuine power might settle staie sure faithe v hitherto therefore wee haue heard saincte peter exhorteth v first girde vp loynes mynde also sincerely walke perfecte faithe consideryng deare price hath co te christe wee haue conuersation feare bearyng selues hold vpon named christias sith god suche iudge respecteth maintes persone one fifte galath rekoneth vp fruites followe faithe fruites spirit saieth loue ioye peace long suffering gentlenesse goodnesse faith meekenesse temperance also doeth saincte peter teache v whiche bee fruietes faithe witte purifie soules obeiyng truthe spirite true faithe bryngeth bodie vnder subiection bridleth lustes fleshe although make cleare riddaunce dispatche thereof ye maker bodie subiect spirite bridle qualifieth wilde motion thereof meanyng also hath sainct paule speaketh fruictes spirite greate busie peece woorke bryng spirite maister beare rule ouer bodie represse wilfull affection fleshlie desire naturally engraffed v parentes possible v liue well state wedlocke without speciall grace saie nothyng wee doe herein beyng without grace saieth purifie make chaste soules rather body surely full well knewe lustes concupiscence fleshe accompainie v graues neuer quenched v although wee bee baptized till diyng daie inough manne conteine hymself acte doyng outwardly chaste virgine harte meane boilyng filthie desire fleshly lustes wee must earnestly endeuour selues diligence soules maie bee chaste chastitie maie proceede come harte soule maie bee continuall enemitie warre naughtie desire still fight againste till cleare deliuered agreeth well added must purifie soules obeiyng truthe spirit muche hath preached spoken chastitie many bookes haue written concernyng aucthours whereof haue taught v long fastyng abstinence fleshe wine suche like quenche filthie motion concupiscence luste whiche although thei helpen therevnto yet could thei sufficient neither could thei beate doune inordinate desire flesh sainct hierom writeth hymself punished pinched bodie euen like ethiopian yet neuerthelesse little therewith profited many tymes dreamed rome companie gentle woman faire maiders bernard also punished suche abstinence almoste spoiled bodie yt stonke loathsomely afore haue declared holy men greeuously tepted outward thinges thei thought thei could restraine quench temptation remedy whiche thei vsed externall outwarde applied outwardlie inwardly deede disease harboured thei could serue sufficient able maister kill desire mynde whiche thei warred peter place sheweth v moste true soueraigne remedie wherewith cure euill witte obedience truthe spirite whiche scripture place also setteth doune esaie faithfulnesse shalbe girdle reynes true cataplasme wherewith reynes girded whose soundnesse must proceede inner thinges outwarde contrariwise outwarde inner soare whiche would cure lieth outwardlie kerther clothes deeyng bredde inwardlie ragingly raigneth lyeth bloud fleshe marrowe veines therefore beste waie outwarde thinges goe aboute represse quenche fleshly concupiscence bodie fasting labour may brought greate debility weakenesse legth thereby vtterly marred spoyled brought vnto death bee cased euill desire faithe able quenche keepe vnder thei shall bee brought giue place yeeld vnto spirite also speaketh prophete zacharie chapter wine whereof christe first drinketh whiche maketh maydens hee drinketh forecasteth arare wine wont enkindle stirre vp naughtie desire wine wit gospell represseth maketh harte chast peter meaneth hee saieth truthe bolden fast harte obedience thereunto giuen spirite none truest cure presentest remedy daungerous euil mischiefe beside none found able driue awaie qualifie euill cogitation vaine thoughtes whe remedie gospell meane entered taken possessio within harte naughtie leude motion straightways giue place vanishe awaie let hym wil trie matter hee shall duely finde bee haue made triall thereof doe well know deuill doth easely suffer man come poinct harte embrace worde god maie feele good taste sauour hath hee knoweth full well great power mightie efficacie subdue beate downe naughtie desire euill thoughtes therefore whiche sainct peter speaketh though thus saie bee desirous remaine continue chast standeth hande embrace shewe obedience truthe spirite saie necessarily behooueth onely reade heare worde god embrace harte therefore enough gospell bee preached heard thou must continuallie cleaue vnto followe grace hath worde oftner man tasteth sweeter still wareth pleasaunter relisheth albeit alwaies teacheth one doctrine concernyng faithe yet neuer bee godlie well disposed mindes sufficiently enough heard addeth apostle loue brotherly without fainyng ende must wee leade chast life ende thereby attaine saluation forsooth ende purpose wee maie serue doe good neighbor shall doe maie restraine keepe vnder sinnes must dutifullie obeye truthe spirite saie faithe woorde god doe bridle keepe vnder subiection sinnes forsoothe maie dooe good others must first bridle ouermaister bodie fleshe spirite shall bee able profite doe good others loue one pure harte feruently holie apostle peter paule doe separate make difference betwene brotherly loue commo loue brotherhood yt bond wherein christian ought among themselues euen brother without respect difference haue common one christe one baptisme one faithe one treasure bee worthie thou whiche thou haste also haue finallie euen riche thou wee haue one treasure sauyng peraduenture receiue worthily thou doest laie vpp gold thou shouldest kepe filthy rag vise cloute therefore wee haue grace christe spirituall blessynges common together also ought haue body liues wealth dignity common one one maie serue others turne necessitie thinges hee verie significantlie saieth loue brotherly without fainyng without glosing hypocrisie dissimulation whiche terme phraze apostle gladlie vse vndoubtedlie thei foresawe wee would sticke call one christian brother yet would falsly feinedly dissemblyngly altogether hypocritically vndermine one haue erected world many fraternity brotherhoodes whiche deede nothing el starke vanity mere deceiptes altogether deuised inuented brought world deuill whiche wholy altogether repugnaunt contrarie faithe sincere loue brother christe aswell myne hee sainct barnardes thine lesse francis thou hearest therefore saie shall come heauen one brotherhood order answere thou thus mere paltrie counterfaited hypocrisie thou speakest christe abide suche trumperie brooke none common brotherhood whiche haue altogether wilt thou plaie notorious foole breakyng erecte make thy self newe vpstart peculier brotherhood truely could well abide thou shouldest erecte one whereby make peculier helpe thy soule certaine number come together contribute gather treasure reliefe bee necessitie therefore christias haue one brotherhood tooke vpon v baptisme whiche brotherhood saincte hath thou looke greate price redeemed great also bought redeemed god bestowed lesse sake greatest saincte sauyng peraduenture embraced treasure better doe saie hath stedfaster stronger faithe furthermore woorde loue hath larger signification brotherlinesse reacheth also vnto enemy especiallie whiche worthie loue faithe sheweth forthe woorkyng seeth nothyng also ought loue see nothing especially exercise operation apparaunce nothyng worthy bee loued rather thynges odious suche maie breede procure loathsomnesse nothyng well liked euen ought effectes loue shewe forthe yea ought also doen feruently saieth peter whole harte euen god loued v suche time wee euery respect moste vnworthie loue beeyng borne anewe thirdlie al thinges therefore performed doen ye saieth borne anewe therefore newe men brought passe owne workes needed newe birthe new man brought forthe power owne worlde must first begotten borne carpenter able owne arte make tree must needes self first grow groud therfore euer made borne sonnes child adam haue naturally sucked synne parentes neither shall wee owne industrie labour euer become child god behoueth v kinde newe birth regeneration therefore meanyng apostle place seeyng therefore newe creature verie meete conueniente withall demeane selues order practise newe kinde life heretofore ye liued hatred vse conuersation loue let thinges transposed tourned sorte came new birthe passe mortall corruptible seede immortall incorruptible woorde god whiche liueth endureth euer kinde seede wee regenerated newe borne otherwise see thynges bee borne generated seede kinde therefore old birth proceeded came seede newe birth also must needes seede seede truely fleshe blood nothing corruptible mortall euen eternall liuyng worde whereby liue whereby nourished haue beyng whereby specially saieth regenerated meanes wont bee dooen brought passe god sendeth worde gospell whiche casteth seede harte menne f seede abide sticke fast harte presently readie holie ghoste fashioneth newe manne whiche becomneth altogether fort afore hath deuises thoughtes cogitation wordes woorkes thus whollie altogether altered whatsoeuer thou aforetyme diddest est huc auoide thou pursuest seekest soeuer thou ste sought thou fleest state corporall generation suche seede whiche manne hath alteration remaineth still seede seede spirite bee chaunged remaineth one euer entirely alteryng chaungyng transmitted altered corruption euill whiche naturally dwelleth quite abolished therefore wonderfull kinde birthe merueilous seede fleshe grasse glorie man flower grasse grasse withereth flower falleth awaie word lord endureth euer place take xl chap esai voice saied vnto prophete crie saied shall crie voice saied crie thus fleshe grasse al glorie thereof flower feeld grasse withereth flower fadeth waie word lorde standeth euer wordes hath peter brought alledged epistle saied bothe riche grounded vpon aucthoritie sondrie scripture meanyng scripture alledged woorde lorde endureth euer whatsoeuer fleshe blood corruptible grasse bee manne neuer flourishyng gallant age bee neuer riche mightie neuer wise iuste neuer braue freshe beautifull whiche appertaine flower yet doeth flower ende wither awaie whiche gallante age beautie lately excelled waxed olde become ilfauoured whiche earst riche growne poore forthe also thinges fade awaie sauyng onely woorde god whiche seede neuer perishe decaye worde whiche preached among though saie neede seeke farre come woorde behold haue euen eye worde whiche wee preache vnto maie qualifie restraine wicked desire thou needest seeke farre onely looke thou gladly embrace preached vnto thee neere vnto thee maie bee heard moses also saieth xxx deuter worde commaunde thee daie farre thee thou shouldest neede goe farre seeke either goe vp heauen goe ouer sea fetche verie neere vnto thee euen thy mouthe thy harte straightwaies preached heard hath feased take full possession thy harte dye vanishe awaie neither dooeth suffer thee dye saueth thee long thou stickest cleauest faste vnto heare iesus christ died bore synnes purchased heauen also hath giuen hath vnto dooe heare gospell glad thynges meane worde god beyng preached whiche peraduenture quickly passeth awaie forgotten bee effectually receiued harte thou throughlie embrace hym faithe slippe thee forgotten truthe creature whatsouer able ouerthrowe gate hell shall neuer preuaile againste yea although sticke faste iawes deuill yet able take holde vpon apprehende woorde muste needes bee bailed deliuered thence shall remaine woorde remaineth therefore without good cause apostle effect saieth none worde bee looked whiche haue preached vnto purpose tendeth whiche paule firste romaine saieth ashamed gospell christe power god vnto saluation beleeue woorde diuine eternall power god although voice sounde speeche dooe quicklie vanishe passe awaie yet kernell saie knowledge truthe contained voice remaineth stil putt goblet iugge wine mouthe drinke vp wine goblet iugge remaining still vnspent also ye word brought vnto v voice descendeth harte beginneth haue life voice remainyng still without vanishyng awaie therefore well tearmed power god yea rather god hymself saied vnto moses exod iiij thy mouthe lxxxj psalme open thy mouthe wide shewe forthe boldlie speake bee hungred fill self beyng present thee speake enough also christe xiiij ihon saieth waie truthe life cleaueth therevnto borne god therefore seede lorde god hymself thinges serue end instruct teache v wee possibly bee relieued holpen woorkes woorde neuer small thyng shewe vttered mouth apparaunce seeme nothyng glorious honorable yet kinde suche incomparable vertue force maketh many child god faithfully cleaue thereunto iohn vpo laied shall euer remaine place hee wil rushe bruise vpon better escape dashed peeces grounde pouder stumblyng offence taking stone whereof scripture speake muche therefore iewes euen daie doe stumble fault owne stone offence stumblyng iewes also dooe wee continually thei greatly boasted name god vaunted themselues bee peculier people god euen fareth v vnder pretext christe churche christe wee renounce renye name christe flatly refuse precious stone hee came worlde among intent thei reiect renounce owne workes thei abiding reiected refused hym euen whiche stumble woorde beyng disobedient vnto whiche thyng thei euen ordeined saied workes good thyng accoumpted god thei neither neither abide hearing therof god hath put christ foundatio vpon thei ought bee laied placed hym attaine al saluation thende thei bee founded laied vpon hym hath caused hym preachyng gospell bee notified declared vnto whole worlde hym thei receiue reiect persiste owne fleshlie sense woorkes thei could abide themselues placed couched vpon christ high pompe dignitie wealthe power would soone quaile abated ye chosen generation royall priesthood holie nation people set libertie hath dignified bee christian true title place hath take vij deuter thus saied iewes thou art holie people vnto lorde thy god lord thy god hath chosen thee bee precious people vnto hymself aboue people vpon earth xix exod saieth ye shalbee cheef treasure aboue people ye shalbee vnto also kyngdome priestes holie nation thou seest peter speaketh saied afore saie still wee must acquaint selues speake priestes scripture speaketh theim let trouble thee thei bee vulgar common sorte tearmeth priestes let euery man god name tearme liste cleaue thou faste vnto woorde god whomsoeuer thou seest hym tearmed called priest lette also bee likewise tearmed called thee giue good leaue greasie rable bisshoppes pope consecrate annoint tearme theim selues priestes name thei thei call themselues priestes god thei able one woorde scripture approoue theim selues thei stiffely mainteine place also vnderstoode spoken answere thou vnto theim afore haue taught thee aske saincte peter speaketh thou shalte quicklie see theim laye theim selues open vnto shame impudencie moste manifest plaine speaketh people christe whole congregation christian saieth chosen generation holie people againe hitherto hath spoken none persones builte vppon corner stone doe beleeue therefore euidently certainly followeth whiche doeth beleeue priest thei shall saie woordes bee taken auncient father haue interpreted expounded therevnto make thou aunswere lette father whatsoeuer interprete thei sainct peter dooeth thus speake vnto hath farre better testimonie warrant god thei haue also elder thei therefore subscribe yeelde vnto hym finallie place needeth interpretation e suche plaine tearmes woordes speaketh theim beleeue seeth monstruously polleshorne greasie popelynges erre faile article faithe therefore wee entrie name thei call themselues whether priestes otherwise wee make care thei call theim selues herein standeth question whether scripture thei called priestes whether god doe name call maie bee chosen appoincted churche execute charge office minister worde feede congregation preachyng administer sacramentes yet neuerthelesse wee priestes many v christian seeyng founded couched vppon stone whiche highest prieste god wee also must needes priestes also whatsoeuer hath haue thesame wherefore would wishe worde priest well name christian bee common name prieste christian baptized one abide popishe shauelynges thus presume take vpon onely good christian onely baptized neither ought suffer thei would onely haue selues bee priestes although notwithstandyng thei haue violently haled pulled worde pertinently properlie spoken vnto theim euen like presumption brainlesse boldnesse thei haue called onely churche whiche pope mured crewe hath hitherto concluded decreed scripture teacheth v maner lesson therefore diligentlie note marke thynges ende thou maiest throughly discerne betweene theim god calleth priestes theim call theim selues meanes long mistakyng wee must length recouer reduce woorde prieste right sense proper meanyng maie bee common name name christian bee priest name outward externall office suche exercised onely towarde god spirite euen self maner wee indifferently called kinges euen priest also kinges place spirituall vocable woordes like also name christian holie churche euen thou doest cal man christian hath muche money wealthe beeyng builte vpon aforesaied stone beleeueth christe likewise art thou therefore called prieste thou haste shauen croune iettest streates long goune thou darest appeare shewe thy self sight god offryng vp thy self vnto hym praiyng whole churche vnto thou bothe canst vsest preache christe verie maner altogether thou arte therefore kyng thou wearest croune golde hast large dominion many people vnder thee subiection thou art lorde thinges yea ouer death sinne hell thou art aswell kyng christ hymself kyng bee thou beleeue hym kyng suche sorte kynges worlde neither weareth croune golde neither rideth pompouslie abroade glitteryng traine gallaunt horse yet neuerthelesse kyng kynges hath kynges vnder power iurisdiction speake thynges must subiect vnder feete behold euen greate suche lorde art thou thou beleeue hym soeuer hath also thyne might peraduenture obiecte thus vnto saie saincte peter thy assertion called christian kynges yet worlde well knoweth kynges therefore saie thei place bee vnderstoode spoken dignitie croune earth deede worlde kyng death hath seized vpon hym shall kyngdome ceasse haue ende shall vnlesse beleeue aright subiecte vnder feete truely beleeue wee place speake eternall kyngdome priesthoode whiche sorte euery one god whiche beleeueth bothe true prieste true kyng ignoraunte knoweth table greasie shauelynges bee nothyng lesse priestes aforesaied polleshorne shauelynges therefore reputed priestes afore god crounes neither god kynges accoumpted kynges thei weare crounes crouned kynges anointed priestes worlde established constituted men pope may holie pleasure make many suche prollyng priestes hym listeth serue turne let presume constitute make priest boldlie maie bee accoumpted prieste god suche doeth god make appoinct therefore sainct peter place saieth bee royall priesthood muche saie christian thou wouldest knowe title power prerogatiue glorie true christian haue thou seest thei bee kynges priestes chosen people priesthood doeth straightwaies ensue shewe forth vertues hym hath called darknesse merueilous light office especially appertaineth vnto priest hee bee ambassadour messenger god according commission hath god sincerely preach declare worde vertues saieth sainct peter wit wonder whiche god hath doen bringyng darkenesse light partes office preache tel forth therein chiefly consisteth office priest thus therefore ende ought preachyng tende one brother declare shewe forthe vnto greate wonderfull worke god admirable vertue christ hath deliuered v sinne death hell misery hath called v vnto eternall life hereof ought admonishe others also thei like sort maie attaine come vnto light vnto ende ought driftes directed first acknowledge knowe god hath doen next diligent care studie notifie preache openly make knowen benefite god towarde wonderfull worke also drawe call men indifferentlie light see men yet ignoraunt hereof ought instruct teache thinges whiche selues haue enstructed taught wit vertue power god thei must obteine saluation attaine merueilous light thou seest sainct peter plainly saieth one onely light wherein maketh apparaunt reason seeme neuer sharpely vnderstande perceiue nothyng el mere darkenesse albeit reason able hath skill coumpt one two three c likewise see discerne knowe blacke white greate small externall outwarde thinges yet able see faithe altogether blinde insomuche wisedome al men worlde gathered incorporated one yet able comprehende reache muche vnto one letter wisedome god wherefore peter speaketh light merueilous light flatlie also telleth euery one u grope darknesse vtter blindnesse god dooe call v true light experience also teacheth v thing heare preached workes obteine thyng god handes therefore wee haue neede mediator make intercession vnto god v reconcile v vnto hym heere doubtlesse must reason needes confesse self neuer able vnderstande know thinges therefore neede light knowledge teache vnderstande therefore whatsoeuer worde god faithe nothyng el blinde darkenesse without two worde god meane faithe reason iumbleth randon groapeth waie like blinde man darke catchyng holde first one thyng neuer knoweth dooe thinges tolde greate learned wise men world thei abide heare thei stamp stare thei fret fume merueilously rage therefore peter sheweth apostle singuler vndaunted boldnesse dared call darknesse whiche whole worlde maner doeth euen generallie almoste adore reuerence light therefore wee see chiefest especiallest office others appertainyng vnto v christian wee shewe forthe declare vertues wonderful workes god vertues notable workes god v doen somewhat afore haue spoken namely christ vertue god hath swallowed vp death deuoured hell consumed sinne placed v eternal life vertues great wonderfull man able comprehende muche lesse perfourme puritie thei wise teache neither haue feelyng yet sounde taste therevpon commeth passe thei speake euen thei thinke within themselues thei comprehende owne reason therefore thei choose bee deceiued concupiscence man doe resiste striue thou bee accumbred naughtie cogitation thoughtes yet bee dismaied neither despaire beware hande thei carie thee captiue remedie teacher doctours haue hitherto taught v wherwith preuent mete inconuenence manne afflict punishe hymself long till foete moe ill thoughtes within hym whiche deuise many naie rather brainlesse persones haue doe vse put practise learne thou lesson thou beyng christian shalt doubtlesse feele thy flesh diuers inordina e lustes wicked motios thou throughly settled fhithe thou shalt assured assaulted thousande wilfull cogitation thousand teptations thou afore stande thou stouttly thy ankerhol plaie man suffer thy self therewith rapri straight way ie againste somm n e replie vnto theim flatte deniall case herein standeth doeth betweene chur waiward housebande vnquiet scouldyng wife euer iarryng murmuryng one againste whatsoeuer liketh one disliketh thus sure note true christianisme thou seest thy self neuer liue quiet neither must thou thinke exempted priuiledged thou shouldst feele siunes within thee feele theim surely thou shalte yet thou must haue suche feeling thou withall yeeld thy consent vnto respect thou must bothe faste praie labour thou maiest better extinguishe subdue thy concupiscence therefore thinke nothyng lesse thou canst bee holie perfecte aforesaied doatying doctours surmize wicte suche one without feelyng sinne within hym long cladd fleshe blood long remaineth synne within v therefore muste euer continuallie striue resiste soeuer hath feelyng hymself man vaine maie boaste christian thei hitherto haue taught v whosoeuer professed monke cleare free sinnes suche one hath neede fight striue sinnes also thei affirme yt baptisme doth ent erly cleanse wash awaie sinnes remnaunt thereof
