honestlie ought magistrate handes receiue praise ought magistrate commende preferre gracifie others example maie bee prouoked drawe allured like vertue integritie thou shouldest thinke reape vnto thy self merde god handes saieth paule rom xiij power bee feared good woorkes euill therefore thou wilt bee without feare power doe well god well doyng ye may put silence ignoraunce foolish men wordes sainct peter schooleth reprehendeth vaine talkatiue person bragge thinke themselues sufficiently furnished euen bare name title christianitie also herein preneteth answereth aforehande obiection perchaunce thei might alledge saiyng faith onely bee sufficient christian workes iustifie purpose neede subiect vnto magistrate paie tribute saieth thus muche although wee receiue good commoditie yet neuerthelesse wee bounde euen god sake freely performe willingly yeeld obedience vnto mouthes enemy god whiche diffame slaunder v maie stopped thei maie able speake bee compelled confesse wee persones harmelesse dutifull obedient sort reade many holie men warrefared vnder heathen prince vaquished subdued enemy thinges subiect seruiceable vnto theim lesse wee bounde yeeld obedience vnto christian magistrate howbeit thought could bee christian liued turkie subiection turke againe maie arise doubt allegation thus christ hath commaunded wee resist euill hym striketh v one cheeke wee turne thei saie bee lawfull v strike kill men answere old obiection ethnickes tymes past alledged christian saiyng thei liue suche order country commonweales would soone bee brought ruine bee quickly ouerrunne wee vnto thinges aunswere thus true christian ought resist euil neither reuenge selues rather suffer violence wrong also cause thei maie chargeable burdenous troublesome ethnikes magistrate inhibited sworde iudiciall tryalles although thei liue orderly hath iust cause complaine vppon thei offer wrong man deserue well men paciently beare whatsoeuer doen others yet false connterfaite christian knowe christe thinges sworde iudgement muste bee vse thei whiche doe hurte wrong others maie punished whereby publicke tranquillitie maie bee maintained godly maie liue peace safetie god therefore ouer beside worde hath instituted appoincted prophane ciuile power represse owne accorde refraine doyng offryng harme iniurie others plainly therefore appeareth god hath appoincted instituted magistrate doe beleeue therefore christian whiche administer function onely maie also ought vse sworde namely thereby releeue neighbour repellyng punishyng malefactours defendyng mainteinyng peace tranquillitie safetie theim bee good vertuous yet neuerthelesse saiyng christe standeth sure resistyng euill although christian man beare sworde whether prince magistrate yet neuer vse hymself neither therewith reuenge hymself priuate quarell owne must execute place office behoofe others woorke christian loue sworde defende whole commonwealthe suffer good men vniustlie molested trodendoune christ gaue bequeathed doctrine theim onely beleeue haue loue suche dooe shewe forth expresse workes seyng greater parte worlde beleeueth neither obserueth precepte commaundement therefore moste expedient ouerrule gouerne theim christias suche thei ethnikes panims staie represse sensuall wilfull outrage otherwise thei bee suffered runne hedlong owne pleasure disordred loosenesse lawlesse violence man bee able liue quietnesse safetie therefore bee twoo sortes rule dominion worlde bee also menne twoo sortes witte christian christian christian gouerned worde god neede respecte selues prophane magistrate thei christian haue neede bee vnder power rule namelie sworde thei abide obedient vnto worde god wee christian obedient gospell wee haue neede sworde ciuile power misseli er malefactours vse punishment sithe therefore bee godlie vertuous christe hath committed euill vnder rule ciuill prophane power thei maie bee gouerned thei ought bee gouerned beleeuers hath reserued vnto hymself gouerneth onelie woorde therefore christian empire principalitie empire worlde neither ciuile prophane power christ yet properlie appertaineth office christ yt externall outward thinge also office condition state men bee beside mere office christe muche infidell miscreaunt maie aswell beare office christian also office sworde neither maketh vnmaketh christian hereof wee haue spoken elswhere oftentymes large free hauing libertie cloke maliciousnesse seruauntes god peculiarlie spoken vnto v haue heard christian libertie yet dooe abuse vnder colour name christ christian libertie dooe commit dooe beste liketh selues libertie breake licencious wantonnesse carnall loosenesse wee see come passe day read haue happened tyme apostle themselues epistle bothe sainct peter sainct paule wee maie manifestlie gather dooen practized whiche adaies greater sorte men vsually committeth wee good gifte greate fauour god dooe againe vnderstande knowe truthe plainly see nothyng mere deceipte iugglyng whiche hitherto pope chergie hath taught established doen conscience thankes bee vnto god deliuered snare humaine tradition freed violence wherein thei entrapped v wee made free tyed vnder paine damnation doe suche thynges thei enioyned commaunded v libertie ought stande maintaine neither suffer selues drawen withall take heede wee make libertie cloake pretext wicked life therefore shamefullie verie vngodlie hath pope dealt behalfe presumyng compell enforce menne lawes christian people neither ought neither bee compulsion good thyng straightwaies decaieth falleth doune faithe christianitie conscience bounde externall rite outward constitution christian must ledde gouerned spirite thei maie knowe first faithe thei alreadie possesse thynges necessarie appertainyng saluation haue neede nothyng el obtainyng thereof nexte knowe thei ought employe addicte industry endeuours nothing el helpe serue relieue neighbour thei maie euen christe hath holpen succoured relieued theim whatsoeuer good thei thus shewe vnto thei doe freely freendly without compulsion thynges maie flowe spryng wel willyng chearfull harte humblie thanketh god praiseth holie name gracious giftes largely bountifully powred vpon vnto purpose serueth saiyng sainct paule j timoth j thus writeth lawe giuen righteous thei suche doe thyng e freely willyngly without either constraint commaundemente thei knowe bee allowed agreable vnto good pleasure god carnall irreligious faithlesse counterfaict christian knowing bondes humaine tradition bee broken hearyng true christian libertie preached come steppyng vaunte themselues iollie christian thei professe themselues obserue keepe pope lawes pretendyng excuse christian libertie thei herevnto tied bound yet meant season omitte leaue vndoen thynges whiche true christian libertie requireth witte chearfull vnconstrained helpyng neighbor thynges vttermoste abilitie without respecte commaundement whiche doe true christian endeuour themselues therefore thei makyng christian libertie onely cloake filthie wicked impuritie doe disgrace pollute precious name excellente title libertie whiche agreeth onely true christian doeth sainct peter place forbid v doe effecte meanyng speech though saie thus although outward externall thynges ye free christian ought compelled lawe obey magistrate law made righteous iuste declared yet ought neuerthelesse doe willyngly vnconstrained necessitie enforced euen loue beare god benefite neighbour read matth vij christ hymself beeyng free lorde notwithstandyng paie tribute polle money also obeyed pilate suffered hymself bee iudged hym whereas notwithstandyng verie place testified saied vnto thou couldest haue power againste excepte giuen thee aboue whiche wordes expressely flattly confirmeth magistracie power yet submitted hymself therevnto pleased heauenly father forcedlie compulsion see peeuishe counterfaites contemnyng aswell thynges please god thynges whiche worlde requireth still persistyng wilfull way corrupte iudgementes haue right vnderstading knowledge christia libertie meaneth brag thei neuer much religio vaunt thei theselues neuer gloriouslie vnder shewes title gospell wee deede freed lawes howbeeit v necessarily required withall wee helpe relieue weake vnskilfull christian brother whiche verie office loue wherevppon sainct paule rom xiij saieth thus owe nothyng man ye loue one therefore would boaste christan libertie muste firste performe doe partes office christian witte loue helpe neighbour afterward vse christian libertie sorte pope whatsoeuer would compell tye hym vnto lawes enioyne hym commaundement dooe maie saie againe sir dooe whiche giue vnto commaundement doe none cause would binde therevnto commaundement taking awaie christian libertie impose necessitie wee must deale doe freely seruauntes god seruauntes men place sainct peter teacheth v man might therby benefite require suche thyng handes willyngly myne owne accorde doe respectyng whether bee commaundement onely consideryng waighyng brotherlie loue requireth handes assuring self thyng right acceptable pleasaunte almightie god suche seruice dueties helpe brother reason cause bee compelled enforced obaie ciuile prophane magistrate yet willynglie myne owne accord obeye thei themselues exact demaunde tendeth serueth commoditie benefite neighbour ende ought woorkes framed thei maie issue proceede willyng louyng mynde thei maie bee profitable auaileable neighbour honour men commaundemente exhortation wee owe honour vnto men although wee bee free libertie ought bee readily benie alwaies doe good doe euill afore wee shewed many place euery christian faithe possessed thynges whiche christes also made become brother therefore euen owe maner honour vnto christe likewise muste honour neighbour thou maiest thinke honour cosisteth outward gesture bowyng doune thy bodie vncoueryng thy heade rather thy harte vnfained sinceritie reuerence hym loue hym highly esteeme hym euen christ hymself bee reuerenced loued highly esteemed moreouer wee temple god sainct paule saieth j cor iij holie ghost dwelleth v wee therefore haue easilie caried leadde superstitious bowyng knee idolatrous hoast thei tearme image woodden crosse wee muche fall doune shewe obeisaunce hym liuely te ple god self maner paule rom xij exhorteth v giuyng honour one goe euery one subiect humble vnto preferre giftes giuen vnto v god vnequall one surmounteth dignitie preeminence place callyng yet man knoweth highest sight god able raise vp hym whiche world abiectest moste seely estate aduaunce hym highest degree therefore euery one though worlde bee placed neuer high callyng ought deiect humble yeeld honour vnto neighbour loue brotherly fellowshippe wee declared afore apostle make greate difference betweene common loue brotherly loue duetie loue euen enemy belongeth comon loue brotherly loue whereby christian loue one euen brother seekyng one oother commodity owne wee haue alike good giftes giuen vnto v god loue whiche sainct peter place peculiarly requireth feare god honour kyng biddeth v onely make greate accoumpt highly esteeme kynges ruler earth withall also honour although thei bee ethnickes heathen whiche thing bothe christ hymself prophetes also prostrated themselues feete kynges babylon might one saie mee loe thou seest place wee ought obey pope euery one ought fall downe prostrate feete aunswere true vsurped tooke vpon hym ciuile prophane power execute place temporall magistrate worldly prince doubtlesse bee obeyed example hee thus saie commaunde thee weare hood shaue thy croune thy head vpon daie faste thou shouldest beleeue god whitt regarded cared parte thereof necessarie thy saluation therefore doe commaunde thee doe beyng ciuile magistrate prophane prince mynded haue dooen hee shall hee doeth plaie tyraunt sore god vicar earth onely vicegerent commaunde thee obserue keepe embrace commaundement otherwise god expresse woordes commaunde vnder paine excommunication deadly sinne maiest thou saie bee fauourable mee sir pope hold excused truely meane nothyng lesse performe dooe whiche thus thou proudely presumptuously commaundest wee bounden bee subiect vnto higher power obeye ordinaunces long thei binde conscience meane long thei impose thyng vppon v concernyng outwarde worldlie thinges yea although thei plaied partes tyrauntes towardes v taketh awaie coate wee commaunded let hym haue cloake also thei entermeddle take vpon raigne ouer spirite leade awa conscience captiue wherein god alone ought sit raigne ought rather offer heades block whit obeye suche poyntes ciuill magistrate externall empier hath power ouer erternall corporall thinges pope hath onely violently challenged vnto hym forcibly intruded vpon externall power outwarde iurisdiction also goeth rake catche chalenge vnto spirituall also whereas deede hath right neither bothe keepeth greate coyle setteth doune lordly commaundements rule lawes ordinaunces apparell choise meates college abbayes priory bishoprikes benefice staieth goeth coyneth bothe synnes good woorkes therefore christ abide suche monstruous empier meane domination externall outwarde gouernement whereby worlde ruled hee bothe liketh alloweth neither vsurpeth entermedleth thyng sinnes good workes spirituall dealinges dealeth altogether externall outwarde policy maintenaunce defence fortification city building making bridge appointyng assessyng tribute receite reuenues mainteinyng continuyng peace defendyng territory landes dominion settyng order punishement malefactours offendours therfore eche christian maie without daunger naie willingly owne accord compulsiuely forciblie ought yeelde obedience vnto suche prince sithens chalengeth authoritie ouer conscience therefore either emperour kyng prince aske mee faithe ought plainly confesse protest vnto commaundement otherwise bounde confesse faithe openly men often occasion offered proceede commaundyng beleeue waie waie muste saie sorte vnto hym noble prince charge respect externall principalitie empire looke well authoritie reacheth encermeddle kyngdome god lawfull eueroache vppon sanie vsurpe vnto self belongeth alone therefore herein maie obeye well abide chalenge right vnto self within dominion yea onely passe rankes watchman setting naught though thei deale hym would saie sure pursue one gunes glaues store partiall prouision think god suffer attempt pull seate set self place sainct peter calleth ciuile magistrate onely ordinaunce man therfore authoritie stretcheth themselues enact commaunde thing vppon statute god poinctes faithe seruants subiect maisters al feare onely good courteous also froward thankeworthie man conscience towarde god endure griefe sufferyng wrongfully praise ye bee buffeted faultes ye take paciently ye doe well ye suffer wrong take paciently acceptable god sainct peter hitherto hath taught v wee subiect vnto ciuil magistrate honour wee ought giue vnto discourse whereof wee haue declared farre extendeth magistrate stretche authoritie limited commission neither ouerrule matter faithe whiche spoken magistrate generall therfore doctrine appertaineth vnto speaketh suche magistracie appertaineth whole comonwealth certaine priuate persones first familie ought bee gouerned seruauntes householde ought demeane behaue themselues towarde maisters meanyng whiche wordes effect seruauntes men woman christian aswell others hauyng one worde one faithe one baptisme benefites besides aswell others therefore sight god nothyng inferiour onely worlde externall teporall life difference respecte thei lesse accoumpt estimation therein beeyng inferiours vnderlinges bounde waite obeye therefore seeyng god hath called estate thei ought frame enure themselues dueties thei shew subiection testifie submission vnto maisters honour reuerence seruiceable vnto carefullie looke dealinges businesse wherevppon prophete dauid psalm cxxiij borowyng apt proper similitude signifieth thereby diligently thei ought attende vnto maisters maistresses eye seruauntes looke vnto handes maisters eye maiden vnto handes maistresse eye waite vpo lord god whiche muche saie seruauntes waiting maiden ought submission feare doe whatsoeuer maie please maister maistresse god requireth therefore thei ought cherefull willyng myndes doe thou thus doest accordyng word god faithe bee assured acceptable allowed god therefore best workes al others man woorke man maie perceiue hee needeth got farre dooe woorkes thy maister commaundeth seruaunt maistresse maide hath god commaunded doen thee think bee bare commaundement man although vttered doen man therefore thou oughtest consider respect maner maister thou seruest whether good badd gentle curteous waiwarde churlish thinke rather maner maister soeuer bee yet duetie truely faithfullie serue hym diligently applie self businesse god sake requireth handes remembryng also lorde iesus christe redemption freedome became seruaunt true doctrine life whiche ought continually bee inculked beaten heades men ala blindnesse age greate nowadaies almoste quight abolished vtterlie extincte doctrine suche sorte none well embrace like sauyng onely true christian haue lesson gospell therefore thou wilt true child god frame thy mynde serue thy maister christe hymself present commaunded thee euery particuler charge doe writeth saincte paule ephe vj seruauntes bee obediente vnto theim maisters accordyng fleshe feare tremblyng singlenesse harte vnto christe seruice eye men pleaser seruauntes christ doyng god harte good seruyng lorde men againe coloss iij ye serue lorde christe oh monkes nunnes adaies state poore seruautes ioye might thei haue conscience giue god thankes benefites neuer one theim truely saie god hath commaunded heare masse sing mattins mumble vp seuen houres suche like trumpery muche one woorde thereof spoken scripture therefore thei bee asked whether thei bee assured doubte profession condition bee allowed god thei aunswere man aske poore moilyng kitchin drudge washeth disshes platter milketh kine yeelde reason saie sir knowe thyng whiche doe acceptable allowed god haue woorde god expresse commaundemente warraunte ought doe thinges surelie singuler comforte excellente benefite right precious treasure whiche man well thinke hymself worthie prince maie thinke hymself happie man highlie god fauour vpon like confidence truste sure commaundement god throughly discharge execute waightie office function truelie maie high callyng doe whiche god hath commaunded namelie punishe transgressours malefactours ala yea seldome happeneth rightly lawfullie able throughlie execute chargeable office condition state seruage thynges sorte poore seruauntes certainly knowe throughlie assured thinges whiche thei doe maisters commaundementes allowed accepted god god respecteth basenesse vilenesse woorke regardeth harte suche vile dradging labour obedient vnto happeneth falleth case al matter vsuallie doeth looke god commaundeth man willyng dooe whiche men establishe commaunde god saie euery one seeketh followeth peraduenture saie haue suche frowarde testie waiwarde angrie maister manne please seruice content whiche sorte fewe euerywhere sainct peter herevnto eth plaine aunswere effecte saie thus thou bee christian bee desirous please god thou must respecte waiward churlishe thy maister consider rather euer beare mynde lorde thy god commaundeth thee therefore thinke thy self well seruice shall serue lorde christe requireth handes bee obedient seruiceable eche respecte duetifull maister bee neuer frowarde sullen vnquiete god commaunde thee wipe shoe errantest verlett deuelishest rakehell worlde thou oughtest chearfull harte willyng mynde doe woorke thyne bee bothe good laudable god woorke whatsoeuer like sorte bee accoumpted right excellent commendable god hath commaunded therefore case respecte persone consider onely good pleasure god willeth bee doen thy duetie seruice sort truely faithfullie performed shall god farre surpasse excell woorkes merites shauelyng priestes mumblyng monkes worlde thei layed together one heape bee thinketh sufficiente pleasaunte acceptable woorke god shall muche auaile vse reason perswade hym nothing better thou doe nothyng worse thou forslowe omite therefore saieth saincte peter must feare bee performed thynges muste orderly duely bee executed seeyng comaundement man god hymself sainct peter doubtlesse place peculierly speaketh suche seruauntes many tyme wit slaues suche country yet daie bought solde like brute beastes euill entreated oftentymes whipped beaten maisters safely without daunger law thei listed might kill put death therefore needefull apostle peter diligently admonishe comfort contented duetifullie serue frounyng waiward maisters beare iniuries thei rigorouslie handeled euery one christian must needes beare crosse pinched iniuries better fareth case therefore take vp kinde crosse willyngly hartely thankyng god verie true affliction pleaseth god profite auaile thee thou arte buffered shreudlie beaten thy desertes thou shouldest boaste bragge sufferyng crosse therevpon saincte peter saieth ye doe well ye suffer wrong take paciently thanke worthie acceptable god true obedience vnto god pleasyng worship behold plainly described set vnto thee true excellent woorkes whiche thou oughtest doe yet foolishemen haue set naught troden vnder feete good wholesome doctrine steede thereof haue deuised founde selues good woorkes inuented owne braines phantasy whiche wee make suche speciall accoumpt thinke neuer sufficientlie enough extoll praise dignifie wee therefore deliuered blindnesse taught againe whiche true right woorkes please god let v handes holden vp heauen yeelde moste humble thankes vnto god greate benefite let v hartily entirely reioyce lorde herevnto ye called christe also suffered v leauyng v example ye followe steppe synne neither guile founde mouthe reuiled reuiled whe suffered threatened committed hym iudgeth righteouslie owne self bare synnes bodie tree wee beyng deliuered sinne liue righteousnesse whose stripe ye healed ye sheepe goyng astraie retourned vnto shepeheard bisshoppe soules herevnto saieth saincte peter ye called vnto forsoothe suffer persecution trouble wrong euen christ self afore hath dooen though thus saie thou wilte bee true follower christe fitte decent agreeable thy profession thou arte iniuried brabble muche repine thereat pacientlie beare take well worth consideryng innocentlie christe suffered thynges sake neither exclame neither cried vengeaunce neither cursed giltleslie brought iudge therfore thou must also looke alwaies bee iustlie dealt withall whollie neglecte care indifferentlie rightlie iustice respect ministred vnto thee thou haste wrong offred thee saie rather thy wrong thanke god herevnto called suffer wrong complaine sithe christe lorde sauiour guiltlesse innocent euery waie complained hath saincte peter alledged certaine woordes liij chapter esaie prophete thus saied committed wickednesse neither guile founde mouthe woordes whose stripe ye healed mentioned also chapter vers v christe pure muche one euill woorde tongue worthie haue honoure handes deserued bee kneeled vnto bee caried armes menne finallie power aucthoritie enough haue reuenged hymself pleased hym suffered hymself rather bee reuiled mocked blasphemed laste put death yet opened mouthe therefore shouldest thou bee whitte vnwillyng suffer persecution wrong sith thou art nothyng synne thou shouldest rather hartilie thanke god highlie extoll gracious goodnesse hath accoumpted thee worthie bee like christe repine mutter bee vnpacient thou art wronged seeyng lorde hymself neither reuiled threatened againe earnestly praied enemy thou wilte peraduenture saie sall allowe thinke well deale iniuriously saie therein thei doe well aunswere saie rather thus thine harte although haue deserued hard dealing bee thus wrongfully entreated yet willyngly suffer thynges lorde god sake beeyng moste innocente sake euill entreated moste wrongfully dealte withall commit thy cause god righteous iudge abundauntly recompence thy sufferynges euen christ committed cause vnto father heauen owne self saieth saincte peter offered vp synnes bodie tree suffered death cause owne sake saluation wee synnes crucified nailed crosse ala wee yet verie farre suche kinde sufferyng wrong therefore thou sincere true christian thou muste imitate christe poincte bee hartily sorie hurte thee praiyng earnestly vnto almightie god maie please hym forgiue theim punishe theim ala thei doe hurte thereby selues soule thei doe harme thee thy bodie thou throughly consider harte rightly waigh thou canst choose presently eased inward grief willyngly suffer thynges pacience finallie wee remember wee selues aswell thei little afore ledde wicked life length tourned vnto christe sainct peter knittyng vp chapter saieth ye sheepe goyng astraye returned vnto sheepherde bishop soules place also hath hee taken esay chapter liij saieth thus wee like sheepe haue gone astraie wee haue tourned euery one owne waie saieth sainct peter wee haue gotten sheepeheard sonne god come doune sake bee sheepeheard bishoppe hee giuyng vnto v spirite feedeth v guideth leadeth v word wee certaine sure saluation therefore thou acknowledge confesse thy sinnes cleane washed taken awaie thou art sheepe hee thy sheepeheard thy bishoppe greatest comfort christian haue thus haue wee fullie finished two chapter epistle wherein sainct peter hath firste laied doune plainlie taught sinceritie faith secondarily sincere workes loue herein also hath hee treated twoo sortes workes namely aswell woorkes whiche wee bounde generalitie shewe vnto magistrate also dueties seruauntes owe vnto maisters sainct peter speaketh seruaunts thesame also appertaineth vnto certaine sortes men namely artificer hirelinges sortes mercenarie seruantes whatsoeuer next laieth downe lesson man wife shoulde christianly liue together third chapter likewise let wiues subiect housbandes euen thei obey worde may without worde bee wonne conuersation wiues thei behold pure conuersation whiche feare whose apparailyng let outwarde broyded haire golde put puttyng apparell let hid man harte bee vncorrupt meeke quiet spirite god thyng much set euen maner time past holy woman whiche trusted god tier themselues subiect husbandes sara obeyed abraham called hym sir whose daughter ye while ye doe well beyng afraide terrour likewise ye housbandes dwell men knowledge giuyng honour vnto woman vnto weaker vessell euen thei heires together grace life praiers bee interrupted finally ye al one minde one suffer loue brother pitifull courteous rendring euill euill neither rebuke rebuke contrariwise blesse knowyng ye thereunto called ye heires blessing man long life see good dayes let refraine tongue euill lippes thei speake guile let eschewe euill doe good let hym seeke peace followe eye lorde ouer righteous eares open vnto praiers face lorde vpon doe euill harme ye followe whiche good notwithstanding blessed ye ye suffer righteousnesse sake yea feare feare neither troubled sanctifie lorde god heartes bee readie alwaies giue answere euery man asketh reason hope meekenesse reuerence hauyng good conscience speake euill euill doer thei maie bee ashamed whiche slaunder good conuersation christe better god ye suffer well doyng euill doyng christe also hath suffred sinnes iust vniust might bryng v god put death concernyng fleshe quickened spirite whiche also went preached vnto spirites prison whiche tyme passed disobedient long sufferyng god abode day noe arke preparing wherein fewe eight soules saued water also figure saueth v euen baptisme agreeth puttyng awaie filth flesh good coscience maketh request god resurrection iesus christ whiche right hande god gone heauen angel power mighte subiect likewise let wiues bee subiecte housbandes euen thei whiche obey word maie without woorde bee wonne conuersation wiues thei behold pure conuersation feare saincte peter place namely speaketh wiues whiche tyme vnbeleeuyng housebandes suche faithful housebandes yet heathen ethnick wiues oftentymes happened day apostle preached gospell emong vnbeleeuyng pagan infidelles emong often seen one party witte either housebande wife conuerted wonne vnto christe still wallowyng persisting errour charge wiues subiection obedience housbandes straightly commaunded muche behouefull necessarie performe shewe forth adaies office therefore wife saieth sainct peter bee loyall subiecte housebande yea though bee infidell heathen inferreth cause conuenient behoouefull doe euen thei whiche obeye worde maie without woorde bee wonne conuersation wiues housebande seeth wife liueth orderly innocently honestlie thereby moued prouoked embrace like christian faithe godlinesse albeeit office preachyng bee committed allowed vnto woman therefore punish sinne dealeth iustly doeth wrong haue deserued doe punishe pardon trespasse offence yet doeth therein iustlie alwaies thinges iustice righteousnesse bee ascribed vnto hym albeit opened better exposition wishe followed verie summe therefore interpretation christe beyng quickened spirite ascended heauen preached afterwarde vnto soules menne afore vsed preache body emong whiche willyngly hearkened vnto menne commonly take greate delight hearyng theim therefore saincte peter bryngeth waie comparison similitude arke noah whereby briefly fewe woordes yet certaine pleasure setteth doune sure lesson confirme faithe whiche setteth doune haue come passe noah made arke sort standeth case euen eight soules saued arke whiche caried vpon water must wee also bee saued baptisme christ churche christ gospell whiche christe preached bodie christe whiche wee hange together faithe deliuered euilles euen noah arke saued beeyng drenched water gene vij thus see example hym brought comprehendeth compendiously briefly bothe faithe crosse life death soeuer bee men whollie depende vpon christ certainly churche christ vtterly drouned killed soeuer v euill issueth commeth old adam whiche also figure saueth v euen baptisme agreeth puttyng awaie filthe fleshe good conscience maketh request god ye hereby satted filth body cleane washed awaie nothyng el cleansed bodie iewes precisely obserued vsed doe suche kinde purifiyng moment force good conscience makyng request god saueth ye feele within good conscience chearfullie confidently daryng shewe self appeare god though couenaunt bargain betweene theim therevppon dare boldly saie hath lorde god promised sure performe suche one deceiue ye thus stedfastly cleaue vnto woorde whollie depende vppon hym misse bee saued meane whereby thus obtaine saluation faithe outward worke selues able way doe resurrection iesus christe small portion woordes hath saincte peter purposely added whiche went shewe reason faithe grounded herevpon christe died descended lower partes staied still anone arose againe deade continued still death remained still miserable estate forlorne wee afore risen againe deade sitteth right hande father hath caused bee published preached vnto v intente wee beleeue hym haue therefore certaine couenaunt promise god vnto whiche wee certainly vnfeignedly dooe truste whiche wee saued preserued euen noah arke thus therefore hath saincte peter laied eye made whole arke spirituall vnto v whiche neither fleshe blood good conscience godward faith whiche right hande god gone heauen angelles power mightes subiecte speaketh make faithe perfecter stronger behooued christe ascende heauen bee made lorde creature power soeuer soeuer bee subiected vnto hym ende might aduaunce bryng v thither make v also lordes thynges whiche singuler force efficacie comfort confirme harte mindes hereby assuredly perswaded thinges christ christ made serue v whatsoeuer power heaue earth yea death deuill hereby enioyned copelled serue v v euen thei bound serue christ lye subiection vnder feete fourth chapter forasmuche christ hath suffred v flesh arme selues like wise mynd hath suffred flesh hath ceassed sinne henceforward liue muche tyme remaineth fleshe lustes men god sufficient v wee haue spent tyme past life lust gentile walkyng wa tonnesse lustes drunkennesse gluttonie drinkinges abominable idolatry wherein seemeth strange ye runne vnto excesse ryote therefore speake thei euill whiche shall giue account hym readie iudge quicke deade vnto purpose gospell preached also vnto dead thei might condemned according men fleshe might liue accordyng god spirite ende thinges hande ye therefore sober watchyng praier aboue thinges haue feruent loue among loue couereth multitude sinnes ye harberous one without grudgyng let euery man hath receiued gift minister one good disposers manifold grace god man speake lett talke woordes god man minister let doe abilite god ministreth god thinges maie bee glorified iesus christe praise dominion euer euer amen dearely beloued thinke straunge concernyng firie triall whiche among proue though straunge thing come vnto reioyce asmuch ye partaker christes suffringes glorie shall appeare ye maie bee glad reioyce ye rayled vpon name christe blessed ye spirite glorie god resteth vpon whiche parte euill spoken parte glorified let none suffer murtherer thiefe euill doer busie bodie men matter manne suffer christian let hym bee ashamed let hym glorifie god behalfe tyme come iudgment must beginne house god first begin v shall ende whiche obeye gospell god righteous scarsely saued shall vngodly sinner appeare wherefore let suffer accordyng god commit soules well doyng vnto faithfull creator forasmuche christe hath suffred v flesh arme worthilie described set doune vnto v moste chiefly labouring builde v faithe teaching v bloud christ sinnes expiated clearely done awaie freed thraldome transgression restored participation eternall set doune excellent secondlie christe giuen set forthe vnto v example patterne v imitate wee haue apprehended taken holde christ free gift faithe wee must nexte endeuour selues bende study imitate alreadie spoken sufficiently suche workes concerne owne body namely wee serue selues bee carefull owne estate faithe wee mortifie sinnes may stroger selues fitter serue neighbour doe tame bridle myne workes seeke wee benefite commoditie neighbour neuer perfectly purged cleane long dwell worlde man feeleth findeth bodie storehouse many euill lustes filthie desire faithe beginneth mortifie sinnes bryng heauenly life yet perfect strong enough doe would euen christe reasoned samaritan yet wholly restored health although woundes bounde vp charge enough giuen curyng looking fareth v whe beleue woundes bound vp saie infection disease propagation deriued v adam begonne bee healed whiche brought passe wee see remisselie slowly speedily quickly accordingly euery one chastiseth represseth flesh hath fuller measure faithe giuen vnto hym therefore haue attained two faithe charitie next studie care ought euen vntill wee dye skowre pourge reliques synne yet harboroughyng within v therefore shalbe called question examination touchyng faithe yea thus maie thei well saie thei brought vnto suche pinch behold christe saieth thus pope saieth cleane contrary christe saieth yea pope saieth naye one submit themselues one well agree menne submit themselues one superioritie gouernement bee bee giuen afore saied vnto bee elder sorte saie peter former sentence spake elder place onely younger sorte ought submitte themselues first elder next one wee take woordes spoken generalitie euen sentence paule rom xij giuyng honour one goyng take place also doe present sentence peter haue reference maner persones indifferently without respecte younger ought obedient submissaunt vnto elder yet elder maie thinke themselues bee lordes ouer readie willyng submitt selues also directed bee yonger theim bee endued deeper vnderstandyng profounder skill thei haue euen old testament lorde oftentymes aduaunced yonglie men beare chief office principalitie sawe theim excell elder wisedome foresight lesson teacheth christ luc xiiij thou art bidden feaste sette thy self doune chiefest place least honourable man thou hidden badde bothe hym thee come saie thee giue man roume thou begin shame take lowest roume thou art bidden goe sitte doune lowest roume c whiche parable concludeth thus exalteth hymself shalbe brought lowe humbleth hymself shalbee exalted therefore truly yonger ought submit themselues bee subiection vnto elder yet neuerthelesse elder ought againe partes bee modestly minded eche thinke hymself harte lowest could thus dooe worlde would bee merueilous quiete staie tranquillitie saieth ought applie selues vnto wee maie thereby shewe forth lowlinesse mynde emplainted resiaunt within v god resisteth proude giueth grace humble bee loftie mynded thei yeelde stoupe god hymself cooleth deiect th contrariwise exalteth aduaunceth humble throwe doune themselues common beaten saiyng euery mannes mouthe would god aswell vsed putte vre life often almoste euery still talked pronounced tongue humble selues therefore vnder mightie hande god forasmuche god requireth ye submit selues see ye doe willingly exalt ye doe vnwillyngly yet shall ye doe abate pride throwe doune loftinesse maie exalt due tyme thinke ye tarie long stedfastly trust ye hym ye haue sure promise hande god blessed though iudgement flesh tyme seeme somewhat long yet neuer haue ye respect tyme committe selues protected gouerned mightie hand god moste assuredly ende exalt caste care hym careth ye haue promise whiche ye maie rest moste perfecte assuraunce god neuer forsake still take care therefore abandon caste awaie owne carefulnesse lette lorde alone deale suffer hym take entier charge care bothe moste comfortable sweete woordes christian conscience moste chearfull amiable vseth many suche forcible prouocations reason perswade humilitie truely nature man stiffe stoute man almoste willynglie abase deiecte hymself renounce owne sensuall phantasy therefore herein suig comforteth v shewyng god dooeth onely looke v also careth bestoweth euen vowelles incomparable loue vpon v bee sobe watche aduersarie deuill roaryng lyon walketh aboute seekyng maie deuoure admonisheth v looke selues goeth open eye wee slumber slouthe giue selues idlenesse regardyng nere bee daunger perill wee maie behold see life worthie apostle hath depainted set vnto v insomuche none hauing conscience touched feare god continually wisheth bee dissolued exchaunge bee kingdome deuill sathan trauailer straunger commeth inne knoweth none theeues murtherers looke well bee carefull owne safetie enter house case bee needes must goe sure neere arme bodie violence fury sleepe muche house stande vppon guarde maie departe thence without harme euen like daunger liue earth sathan beareth swaie prince hath harte men within daunger power bryngeth passe whatsoeuer listeth terrible matter thinke thereon therefore peter herein giueth v watchworde beware admonisheth v carefull diligent looking selues saiyng ye sober giuen drunkennes surphetting swine care nothyng bellie fitte nothyng good therefore wee must endeuour selues haue alwaies readinesse armor sobrietie watche ye saieth onely spirituallie also corporallie heauie lumpishe drowsie body hath pampered crammed ingurged self meates drink fit able resist deuill seing hard enough doe strong faith haue plentifull giftes spirite cause wee muche giue selues sobrietie watchfulnesse saieth hee aduersarie deuill skuddeth like roaring lion seeking maie deuour deuill neuer sleepeth throughly enured furnished guile suttletie malice carieth cancarde stomack v leaueth waie vnattempted maie molest ensnare v yea well knoweth whiche waie laie baytes catch v bryng v vnto lure therfore roameth trudgeth vp downe like roaryng rampyng lyon yelleth roareth hideouslie horribly though would deuoure commeth waie therefore hath sainct peter left vnto v writyng necessarie profitable admonition wherein discouereth vnto v deadly infernall enemie wee take heede hym paule bee ignoraunt malicious driftes skuddeth walketh drift meanyng thereby bryng v negligence securitie wherein maie lulle v straightwaies issue budde thence anger wrath contention arrogance shamelesnesse contempt god mischieues whatsoeuer note saieth deuill walketh setteth vpon thee directly thy face knoweth thou art fenced garded cowardly lyeth waite surprize thee behinde thy backe aslope one side pryeth tooteth within thee without thee diligently espie thee vauntage maie set vppon thee hath attempted thee one waie speede purpose straightwaies taketh hande misse purpose side thee flingeth omitting suttle deuise craftie ambush cunnyng pollicie catche thee trippe possesse thee finde thee strongly armed fenced one parte planteth batterie side bee disappoincted chargeth vpon thee incredible speede place neuer ceasseth cotinuall practise mischiefe thy ouerthrowe confusion neuer taketh pause staie still runneth suffryng thee haue maner test intermission yet wee men senselesse carelesse make reckonyng geare neither watche wee withstande hym whereby maie easilie without resistaunce assaile ouerthrowe v let euery one therefore looke diligently warely hymself shall finde true thei haue tempted bee ignoraunt therefore wee twise miserable liue carelesly retchlesly would enter cosideration selues life present see good cause v crye call help none otherwise wee beset nuber murtherous theeues caused iob saie life man earth mere warfare continuall temptation fight ye saie doth god place v life beeyng full misery truely cause faith maie exercised encreased gladder willinger departe hence death might become sauoueie vnto v bee earnestlier v desired resist stedfast faithe wee must bee sober watche yet ende body maie bee fit readie conflict battaile yet sufficient ouercome deuill withall weapon onely auaileable respect bodie maie bee lesse occasioned sinne true weapon wherewith wee must giue ouerthrowe foyle eenemie faithe wee take sure holde god worde harte constantly cleaue therevnto faithe deuill shall neuer bee able vanquishe v like daunced cowarde straight way runne fielde thou canst saie hath lord god spoken stedfastly beleue hereupon staie self hereunto doe leane thou shalt see deuill quickly like micher sneake awaie departe beautinesse ill concupiscence iuste wrath couetousnesse fainthartednesse desperation vanishe packe awaie also suche uctletie craft deuill hardlie suffer thee come poynct vse meanes hee plucke weapon thy hande whiche easily bryngeth passe hath ensnared thee drowsie slothfulnesse made thy bodie vtterly vnapt battaile giuen nothyng el lasciuious wantonnes meanes little adoe wringeth thy hande sworde spirite worde god firste graundmother eue word god wherevnto firmely stedfastly adhered shee fallen deuill sawe hee spurned ill thought though heresie errour man zeale truthe preache tell sectes bee contrarie doctrine laied downe gospell thei carie men awaie faithe workes thei straightwaies open mouth crye saie deliberation dispensation forbiddyng whiche christe plainly allowed makyng bee sinne sinne yea whosoeuer bee speaketh blasphemous treachery enormious prankes shalbe sure bee condemned burned ash waie truthe right vertuous life syncere conuersation without halting hypocrisie truth beeyng onely sett downe worde god faith firmely beleeued waie wherein true christian ought walke waie truth fellowes wise abide blaspheme reuile slaunder condemne ende maie establishe extoll magnifie mainteine peeuishe pedlarie owne shamelesse sectes couetousnesse shall fained wordes make marchandise couetousnesse moste parte companion heresie sower fa e doctrine generally haue chiefest respect vnto bellie day hath manifestly seen none would either patter masse mumble vp vigiles thei called without money among peine pa er oster colledge monasterie freerie erected peopled till order taken maintenaunce euen riotously abundantly neither house god sake onely would doe thyng man money must without dealing purse penilesse nothyng bee gotten handes pitifull lurdaines holie maisters true faith beginneth preached little money stirryng bryngeth stoare penny downe goe pilgrimage bulles pardon bee bought man abbayes nunnery esteemed vpon whiche notwithstandyng halfe wealth christendome bestowed profite redoundyng commyng thereof man sauyng onely greasie priest munkes freers nunnes way meanes doe thei thus scrape together rake themselues muche money fained woordes saieth peter shall make marchandise haue coigned certaine smooth speech serue turnes whereby cozen men money thei saie thou wilt bestowe many hundreth crounes vppon blessed ladie vpon sainct thou shalt therein doe merueilous meritorious woorke thou shalt buye therewith many pardon many thousande yeres thou shalt haue cleare remission thy sinnes finally thou shalt deliuer many thy freendes soules purgatorie c suche like wordes deuised feigned none purpose picke men purse gleane money triflyng trashe thei sell deare withall thei scratch together suche huige summes money mite merite grace remission sinnes muche soeuer boast wrest holie precious worde god bleare eye worlde serue auaritious appetite also sacrament blessed bodie bloud forthe described holie romishe clergie vsuall property whose iudgement long agone farre damnation sleepeth iugglyng paltrie peter meaning shal alwayes cotinue iolitie neither shal thei choppe chaunge madnesse shalbee euident men thei maie confounded god open eye graunt grace turne vnto hym true earnest repentaunce forsake detest wicked fruictlesse sectes sith maie learne nothyng el sectes perdition condemnation albeit bee altogether peruerted desperatelie seduced sectes yet sectes themselues nothyng el vndoubted certein sect damnable perdition sorte therefore hath peter described filthie wicked life popish monster sawe would come passe syncere doctrine gospel preached yt apostle laieth eye three straunge terrible example god hath condemned iustice punished wit aungelles whole worlde city sodome gomorrhe god spared angel sinned cast downe hell deliuered chaines darknes kept vnto danation word peter terrifieth liue securitie wilfully wallowe wickednesse see whiche bee pope sworne suppliantes deepely drowned dregges filthy tradition thei looke bigge vaunt theselues impudentlie though thei would treade thei liste vnder feete peter therefore place speaketh purpose hee say meruailous malapert saucinesse presumptuous boldnesse thus impudently seeke establishe maintaine force violence heilishe impietie though thei thought god awe theim would spare winke theim spared greased popelynges romishe route disciple fauourers abetter sectary verie child balaam hee gaue pestilente counsell erecte set vp idoll worshipped whereby israelite beeyng drawen synne prouoked vengeaunce wrathe god greeuously punished thesame death many thousandes euen like maner bisshoply balaamites haue erected idoll vnder name god witte owne peeuishe tradition lowsie inuentions doctrine merites iustifiyng woorkes excludyng banishyng fatther thus thei steale awaie mennes conscience cause leaue true liuyng god goe whoryng vnto straunge idolles whiche rebellion disobedience hath prouoked god wrathe indignation hath long punished worlde suche greate blindnesse obstinacie wherein many soule hath perished al whiche misery mischiefes wee maie thanke none graunde spirituall lordynges saincte peter therefore peculiarly properly resembleth likeneth false teacher vnto balaam prophete like dooe thei money sake bryng moste abhominable id latrie destroie infinite number soules verie interpretation name prophete maketh somewhat better openyng matter bileam balaam hebrue tongue signifieth deuourer sweepestake supper vp open mouthe deuoureth gulleth vp cometh hand beastly odious name therfore giue vnto hym allured cause many men sinned whereby thei brought deathes destruction suche maner fellowes balaamites clergie romishe sinagogue day wide ope throates verie deuilles dououryng swallowyng vp innumerable soules sirname prophete sonne bosor whiche signifith fleshe moses calleth hym beor whiche signifieth foolishe likewise polleshorne doltes blinde blockish foolishe seekyng beare rule ouer others haue moste neede themselues ruled gouerned others suche bee menne begotten fleshe spirite beegetteth maner persones thus hath god scripture properly aptly tearmed sette liuely colour namely thereby giue v vnderstande knowe bee thought asse beeyng dumme beaste daiely accustomed yoke burdes signifieth people whiche must bee content bothe bee snaffled brideled sadled ridden vpon goe whiche waie thei bidden asse violently dealt withall greeuously beaten went waie forced goe still forwarde till came suche straite lane shee could waie either starte aside narownesse place goe angell withstoode stopped driuen fall doune poore people often thei feele theim selues hardly dealt withall caried vnsuffe able errours faine would goe aside wicked waie straighwaies seducyng balaamites readie rigour violence bryng erring waie againe therein compelled enforced goe till pleased god open mouthes putte woordes therein name praised euen young child doe talke whereby brainsicke madnesse notoriously detected though thei moste shamelesse impudent yet thei choose blushe thereat place balaamites maie fitly bee answered thei bragge crie accordyng wonted order meete laie people thei call read scripture talke conferre one rather giue eare hearken generall councelles doe decree soeuer thei agree vpon onely bee beleeued embraced maie thus answere god speaking poore asse reprooued prophete whiche satte backe madnesse thei therefore beeyng infatuated harte whollie possessed couetousnesse marueile though god stirre vp poore common people declare shewe foorthe truthe thei hitherto haue surcharged heauie burdeins driuen whiche waie thei lifte none otherwise dumme seelie asse seruyng onely carie burden therefore similitude sainct peter sheweth betweene balaam blinde popishe guide welles without water cloudes caried tempest solomon xxv prouerbes vseth similitude saiyng manne boasteth false liberalitie like cloudes winde without raine saieth sainct peter place thei welles without water cloudes caried tempest boaste great thing thei performe nothyng thei like welles stopped dried vp hauyng water yet thei beare theimselues highly vppon title boste themselues bee true welles scripture calleth theim welles whiche teache doeth flowe issue good wholesome doctrine wherewith soules men maie refreshed office thei ought doe thei appointed ala sauyng onely name suche thyng theim likewise thei call theimselues shepeheardes whereas verie deede thei rather rauenyng wolues againe thei cloudes caried hither thither winde thicke blacke cloudes destill droppe doune raine vpon earth thinne light fleetyng cloudes aire whiche tossed caried hither thither commeth raine euen likewise doe pompous prelate vaunt bragge carie loftie high countenaunces churche seducyng worlde owne vaint guegawes tradition beyng like light windetossed cloudes contented swaie whiche waie soeuer sathan lifteth carie preache soeuer maie likyng much one worde pure sincere gospell god gospell word none preacheth thei true preacher teacher therefore thei v esaie place scripture tearmed cloudes thei doe destill lette fall harte auditorie sweete comfortable water god truthe mercie blacke darknesse reserued euer liue euen pleasure euery thing accordyng owne harte desire prospereth hath good successe glommie daie toward shall come vpon euerlastyng darkenesse although thei neither beleeue feele speakyng swelling wordes vanitie beguile wantonnes lustes fleshe cleane escaped whiche wrapped errour ye aske bee called welles without water cloudes without raine sith thei preache much euery peter maketh answere thei preach deede rayne enough enough preachynges nothyng el swellyng proude woordes wherewith accloye fill eares poore seelie people thei make beleeue thei speake right good catholike whereas indeede nothyng vaine fonde childishe thus lubberly monkes wont braue plausible word boaste vaunt obedience pouertie chastitie thei would thought common people menne holiest whereas doings preachinges nothyng mere iugglynges deceites collusion hauyng theim either faithe charitie also loftie vaine bragge state office bishoppe estate perfection whereas thei bee mitred state dooe nothyng pompously ieste streates awaited vppon greate retinue suiters seruauntes though great lordes fare like prince riding vpon braue horse like gallant caualieres without regard pastorall charge sauyng thei hallowe churche consecrate altar baptize belle suche like swellyng vaine wordes whole pontificiall law full thwackte pestred thei beguile wantonnesse lustes fleshe cleane escaped whiche wrapped errour drifte welles teacher none entangle catche snare selie soules scarcely afore escaped namelie child lately baptized newly receiued church washed synnes deliuered adam engraffed christ saie waxyng somwhat bigge thei lye awaite ensnare drawe errour thei ought rather teache principle groundes faithe charitie beare crosse christ ala thei instill nothyng tender myndes praise hypocriticall woorkes whereby commeth passe thei seelie younglynges caried backe againe errour although afore thei escape thence doe thei thus beguile men wantonnesse lustes fleshe baites dooe thei vse accomplishyng thereof forsooth holie priestes monkes freers nu ne reste marked mate dooe saie teache theim thei ought marie liue single life vnto whiche thei binde theim faste vowes preceptes whiche dooyng thei clogge beguile menne incensyng incityng theim lustes fleshe wherein thei suffer theim miserably burne without allowyng vnto theim lawfull remedie whiche god hath ordeined wee see peter speaketh none false teacher bussardly guide whiche aflote raigne like prince churche god ouer poore baptized beleeuyng christian promisyng vnto libertie themselues seruauntes corruption soeuer manne ouercome euen vnto hee bondage thei extoll praise vaunte holie order religious sectes sinnelesse profession whiche soeuer doeth enter shall bee saued moste swinish impudent dominicane thomas writeth affirming soeuer professeth hymself moke state perfection wherein tyme whe newlie baptized thereby shall assuredlie merite ioyes heauen haue full remission sinnes owne workes suche like blasphemy must wee listen giue eare vnto beeyng nothyng ashamed compare owne dirtie dreames triflyng toyes vnto faithe baptisme whiche bee god owne proper woorkes institution hauyng spirite god hym hearyng horrible blasphemy suffer holde peace suche like madde conclusion impious sentence monkes doe traine vp youth withall finallie whiche least poinct meruailed theim aucthours detestable errours thei haue canonized saincted whereas theim bee true sainctes deede thei haue murthered burnt ash haue escaped filthinesse worlde knowledge lorde sauiour iesus christe yet entangled againe therein ouercome latter ende worse beginnyng sainct peter heere proueth sheweth reason thei seruauntes corruption knowe christe throughly truely knowe wit onely sauiour redeemer owne mere goodnesse grace hath freelie pardoned forgiuen v sinnes knowledge wee escape iniquitie deliuered filthinesse worlde whiche corruption filth hauing baptisme renounced put againe myered throwne hedlong whensoeuer departe start faith trust owne vile work faith faileth absent spirit present spirite wantyng nothing fleshe cleannesse bee sort hath fallen hitherto churche rome first hearkened vnto embraced pure gospell afterward declined turned aside bypathes ma deuised doctrine swarmeth al maner abhominations become common synke blasphemous impietie latter ende thereof therefore farre worse beginnyng become farre desperate forlorne ethnikes euer heard worde god better haue knowen waye righteousnesse haue knowen turne holy commaundement giuen vnto come vnto accordyng true prouerbe dogge returned owne vomit sowe washed wallowyng myer prouerbe hath peter taken booke prouerbes solomo hath word dogge turneth againe owne vomite foole turneth foolishnesse prou xxvj also baptisme thei haue forsaken wickednesse washed cleane filthie life haue taken themselues co conuersation faithe charitie afterwarde fall backe infidelitie trust owne workes myere deraye themselues againe filthinesse formed place therefore ought wise bee applyed workes papistes vse doe auriculer confession shrift wont thus enioyne whose confession thei heard take heede hencefoorth thou bee chast milde gentle pacient c thei ought rather thus enstruct teache thou haue desire become vertuous godlie humbly praie vnto god hartie earnest praier would please hym graunt vnto thee true sincere faith thence beginne liue godlie departe wickednesse impietie thou art possessed true sincere faith good work straightwaies followe issue shalt thou liue chast pure remedie none ridde thee daunger synne although whyle thou mayest hide restraine wickednesse impietie thyne harte yet burst open flame length seconde chapter seconde epistle wherein apostle hath forewarned foretolde v maner teacher false seducer afterward come among v miserablie misleade v pretend excuse haue sufficient warnyng aforehand howbeit wee haue little regarded therefore fault greater wee haue thus sleightly esteemed gospell swerued sweete doctrine comprized whereby wee haue lewde liues prouoked heauier wrath god v wee vnwillyng heare pope lubberly drone bee inueighed againste monstruous marchandize christian soules bee condignely taunted reproued v taketh occasion thereby amende owne life refourme former conuersation tryfling matter laughyng toye serious case greate importaunce suche whereat harte ought tre ble sent vnto v god plague wickednesse impietie paule witnesseth ij thes ij saieth receiued loue truth might bee saued therefore shall god sende strong delusion beleeue lye punishment reuenge god extended perishing onely false counterfaite seducing teacher theselues might haue seemed tollerable hauyng maistered ouerruled whole worlde pleasure haue caried hell whole multitude people haue beene bewitched enchaunte spirituall sorcery remedie therefore v recure mischiefe prostrate selues mercie seate almightie god feare humilitie moste penitently confessyng faultes suppliauntlie imploryng diuine grace assistaunce might please vouchsafe remoue take awaie plague v earnest hartie praier wherewith wee must impugne withstande false deceiptfull teacher sathan aduersarie deuill bee driuen awaie weapon booke declared latter daie men fall suche grosse deuilish errour denye god mocke deryde thei heare preached christe domesdaie saiyng true whence soeuer borowed ought straictly bee taken though whole world fall suche generall apostacie vniuersally blaspheme god greater parte portion thereof fall awaie see plainly come passe dailie burst gospell shall published openly preached among men many wicked shall wraie themselues inward harte many shalbe openly detected whose wickednesse impietie secretly lurketh dissimuled number adaies small beleeue little nothyng latter daie neither thinke euer come suche mocker skorners peter forewarneth v tellyng v sundrie whiche would think none life therfore would passe day lewdely inordinately accordyng deuises sensuall lustes deede rome italie prophesie long ago fulfilled thei come thence v bryng opinion filthie wicked life leade doe teach v country chaunce inhabite little latter daie suche maner men must needes bee christe foretolde matth xxiiij dayes noah likewise shall commyng soonne man day floud thei eate drinke marie giue mariage euen vntill daye noah entred arke knew nothing till floud came tooke awaie shall also commyng sonne man litle case hitherto hath straunge thyng shall happen sainct peter therefore forewarneth v bee lightly caried awaie wicked speech rather knowe thei bee vndoubted signes token daie come verie shortlie willingly knowe heauens old earth water water woorde god wherefore worlde perished ouerflowed water thei suche peruerse frowarde persones saieth thei disdaine grudge bestowe tyme labor learnyng truth separated fro water beginnyng made woorde god againe earth whollie ouerflowed drouned water menne liued secure carelesse thei looked harme come vnto theim neither thought destruction hande yet sodainly floud couered theim whiche peruerse froward persones willyngly wilfully ignorant plaine meanyng woordes saie god destroied worlde water terrible example declared able droune vniuersallie muche destroie hauyng muche often plaine sundrie wordes many seuerall place threatened promised thesame heauen earth beginnyng creation woorde god thei euerlastyng water rested aboue cloudes firmament separated water whiche sea riuers vpo earth belowe earth ouerwhelmed surrounded deepe worde god parted water became drie lande standyng beeyng hemmed water whiche moses large describeth saint peter lightly touched worde god whereby thei made created thynges therein preserued gouerned nature stande remaine suche situation therefore god vnspeakable power vpholde preserue gouerne theim thynges would quickly come wrecke ruine bee sonedrenched couered wholly ouerflowed water mightie thee worde whiche god spake whe saied lette water vnder heauens bee gathered one place let drie lande appeare let water depart aside giue place drie lande maie bee seen menne maie dwell thereon otherwise saied afore nature water would ouerflowe couer whole earth whiche commeth passe straunge miracle among woorkes god saieth sainct peter wilfull flouter stiffenecked deriders peruerse incosiderate thei maliciously thinke skorne shewe honor holie ghost reade scripture therein see god keepeth preserueth gouerneth worlde within water wherby thei might well perceiue see thynges handes god therefore sithe hath alreadie destroied world bringing therevpon general deluge also pleaseth doe vnto v example thereof ought greatly mooue eche one v performed whiche afore threatened none otherwise think surely abide woordes doe whiche hath spoken concernyng v heauens earth whiche kepte woorde stoare reserued crept whiche old ordained condemnation vngodlie men thei whiche tourne grace god wantonnesse deny god onely lorde lorde iesus christ therefore putt remembraunce forasmuche ye knewe lorde deliuered people egypt destroied afterward whiche beleeued angelles also whiche kept first estate lefte owne habitation hath reserued euerlastyng chaines vnder darkenesse vnto iudgement greate daie sodom gomorrhe city theim like maner thei comitted fornicatio followed strauge flesh set forth ensample suffer vengeance eternall fier likewise notwithstadyng dreamer also defile fleshe despise gouernement speake euill theim aucthoritie yet michaell archangell stroue deuill disputed aboute bodie moses durste blame hym cursed speakyng saieth lorde rebuke thee speake euill thynges whiche thei knowe whatsoeuer thynges thei knowe naturallie beastes whiche without eason thynges thei corrupt themselues wo bee vnto thei haue followed waie cain caste awaie deceipt balaams wage perisheil gainsaiyng core spottes feastes charitie thei feast without feare feedyng themselues cloudes thei without water caried windes corrup tree without fruit wise dead plucked vp rootes late ragyng waues sea fomyng owne shame thei wand yng staires reserued blacknesse darkenesse euer enoch seuenth adam prophesied suche saiyng behold lorde commeth thousandes sainctes giue iudgement men rebuke vngodlie emong wicked deedes whiche thei haue vngodlie committed cruell speakynges whiche wicked synners haue spoken hym murmurer complainer walkyng owne lustes whose mouthes speake proude thynges hauing mennes persones admiration avantage ye beloued remember woordes whiche spoken apostle lorde iesus christ thei told bee mocker laste tyme whiche walke owne vngodlie lustes maker sectes fleshely hauyng spirite ye beloued edifie selues moste holie faithe praiyng holie ghoste keepe selues loue god lookyng mercie lorde iesus christ vnto eternall life haue compassion puttyng difference saue feare pullyng fier hate
