cleopas sister blessed virgin marie mother christ ioh xvj appeareth expressely bee written iude apostle heerein hee speaketh maketh mention apostle though hee one disciple written certaine yeares neither conteineth speciall peculiar matter maie well fullie bee gathered afore going second epistle peter vnto hath entier reference al reason saiynges maner taken conclude nothing el epistle directly painetyng poinctyng abuse fleightes treachery papisticall clergie beloued gaue diligence write vnto common saluation needefull mee write vnto exhorte ye earnestly contend maintenaunce faith giuen vnto sainctes effect meanyng could choose write vnto admonishe exhorte persist manfully gooe forwarde faithe whiche hath preached vnto saie needefull necessarie put remembraunce striue al endeuour continue perseuere right waie cause needefull necessarie followeth certaine men crept whiche olde ordained condemnation cause haue taken hande admonish perseuere continue faith whiche ye haue heard euen creepyng alreadie entred certaine false seducer deceiptfull preacher whiche goe teache sowe among counterfaite doctrine contrarie rule faith whiche ye haue soundly learned take ye heede therfore suche mischieuous flye generation thei suttlie sodainly steale waye men conscience erroneous tromperie seduce eatie right waie truthe perceiue bee ware fetchyng collusion saied peter afore shalbee among false teacher c iude saieth long agoe foreordained codemnation iudgement thing easie v vnderstande knowe man iustified owne woorkes faithe onely christe assuredly faithfully beleeueth staieth vpon chief buttresse onely piller safetie made partaker al benefites christes workes faith become sure groundworke faith layed workes wee able doe ought tende benefite commoditie neighbour workes euer wrought ende deuilishe damnable let man therefore diligentlie take heede dealeth lette hym direct woorkes fruictes liuely faith helpe benefite neighbour al odious abhominable sight god sorte vowed profession meriting woorkes massyng priestes mumbling munkes therfore carieth men ankerholde faithe bables lowsie ceremony greasie votary woorkes deceiuer seducer draweth men like daunger condemnation vngodlymen whiche turne grace god wantonnesse preachyng whiche opened vnto v grace god wherein christ set foorth commended vnto v hee good benefites exhibited freely giuen vnto v wee cleerely freed deliuered sinne death hell miserie free grace gift saie thus offred vnto v gospell seducyng false deceiptfull hypocrite dooe abuse maintenaunce themselues lasciuious wantonnesse beare themselues bolde vnder name christian b ast prate muche gospell liue dissolutelie disorderlie dooe thynges accordyng pitche owne wilfull affection lawlesse lustes spendyng tyme ry banquettyng carowsing gluttonie vaunt bragge saiyng thei haue taken vpon spirituall kinde life vtterly renoued delightes seculer state worldly dealynges whereas vnder vizarde pretended simplicitie thei haue inuaded raked handes maner wealthe delites dignity worlde alreadie saieth iude begunne bee put practise wee reade mischiefe bishoppes seeking lordly authoritie higher prerogatiue christian beganne aboue thousande yeares agoe whiche thyng epistle hierome euidently bee seen deny god onely lorde lorde iesus christ also writeth sainct peter christ deniyng mouthe outwardly woordes thei confesse god lord woorkes dealynges thei flatly deny lorde christ acknowledgyng hym bee lorde chalenge rather lordinesse predenimation vnto themselues thei preache fastyng pilgrimage buildyng abbaies chastitie obedience pouertie suche like right high waie felicitie thei th miserablie seduce drawe men truthe wretched workes vtterly suppressyng concealyng keepyng christ doune lesse thei saie christ auaileth nothyng neither woorkes fire whitte helpe thee thou must needes trust thy self merite heauen thyne owne workes thus thei ny lorde hath bought redeemed v owne precious bloud peter afore declared therefore putte remembraune muche ye onto knewe lorde deliuered people aegipt destroied afterward whiche beleeued angel also whiche kept first estate left owne habitation hath reserued euerlastyng chaines vnder darknesse vnto iudgement greate daie sodome gomorrhe city aboute whiche like maner thei committed fornication followed strange fleshe sett forthe ensample vengeaunce eternall fier inferreth three seuerall example whereof two last metioned peter one onely addeth child isral god many wonder brought lande egipt vnbelief dyed wildernesse destroyed sixe hundreth thousande men beside woman child vnder twentie yeares came egipt left moe onely twaine num xj example bringeth admonition terrour hee saie let called name christian vnder colour thereof turne grace god wantonnesse take heede looke well themselues least happen vnto whiche light vppon israelite truely since tyme blind poperie beganne clere light gospell couered restrained beeing publiquely preached one plague hath still fallen necke whereby god hath still tyme tyme taken reuenge vnbeleeuers giuen ouer iawes sathan likewise notwithstandyng dreamer also defile fleshe doctor teacher calleth dreamer one dreameth thynketh haue somewhat see many thynges whiche truth vaine phantasy awaketh seeth haue nothyng perceiueth bee dreame maketh accoumpt thereof whatsoeuer iuggling rabbines lordly maisters doe saie nothyng mere dreames whiche shall one daie eye shalbee opened well finde know haue nothyng namely thei goe perswade men shauen crounes forked cappes wilfull pouertie counterfaite chastitie vowed obedience suche like trashe guegawes thinges acceptable vnto god herein merueilouslie blea themselues owne imagination thinke themselues see whiche deede false phantasticall better fonde foolishe dreame truthe trashe tromperie god nothyng el mere dreames lye therefore callyng dreamer wel hit home right name dreames seduce beguile bothe themselues worlde vice liuyng looselie wantonlie apostle doe peculiarly attribute ascribe whiche bee greazed priestes marked baalamites god long agoe foretolde v bee sect liuyng without wiues daniell also prophecying kyngdome pope foretolde long agoe lust vpon woman dan xj foresawe thei would suche could abide bee linked lawfull mariage woman burne lust wicked concupiscence one outwarde iolie vertues muche vnlike inwarde property namely dreamyng sleeper despise gouernemente speake euill aucthoritie third qualitie thei refuse bee subiecte temporall sworde ciuile magistrate wee knowe teache long wee liue vppon earth wee bounde worde god yeeld obedience vnto magistrate faithe christe doeth violate infringe disanull externall pollicie therefore lawfull man exempt hymself obedience toward wherevpon see plainly consequently prooued pope canon decree touchyng ecclesiasticall immunitie bee nothyng verie deuises inuentions sathan yet michael archangell whe stroue deuill disputed bodie moses durst blame hym cursed speakyng saied lorde rebuke thee one place whiche epistle old father allowed receiued canonicall alledgeth example whiche read el place within whole bodie bible namely michaell archangell contended deuill bodie moses contention thinke grewe herevpon many notable story written moses namelie laste deuter wee reade angell god buried hym man knoweth sepulchre vnto daie againe scripture testifieth hym chapter arose prophete israell like vnto moses lorde knewe face face c seyng therefore greate estimation reuerence moses among iewes interpreter expositor write vpon laste chapter deut saie moses buried god sepulchre neuer hitherto knowen founde man whiche god intente iewes bee kept occasion committyng idolatrie whereinto thei might easily quickly haue slipped thei bodie noble renoumed prophete emong theim moses wherevpon thei gather contention mentioned iude arose deuill would gladly haue bodie moses bee manifestly knowen intent people might haue occasion committe idolatrie thereby ministred vnto albeit michael archangell yet durst saieth iude rebuke hym cursed speakyng railyng sentence blasphemous mouthes peruerse persones ashamed despise treade vnder foote speake euill power whiche ordained god curse theim eight ninth generation whereas thei themselues nothyng el wretched caitifes seelie fraile creature yet see thei michael one chiefest angelles afraied curse raile vpon deuill beyng moste wicken spirite daryng saie farther lorde rebuke thee speake euill thinges whiche thei knowe soeuer thynges thei knowe naturallie beastes whiche without reason thynges thei corrupt themselues kinde persones cursed speaker blasphemous railers thei haue skill nothing excommunicatyng accur ng deliuering ouer satha onely kinges prince potentate power euen god hymself blessed sainctes bull supper lorde seen thei knowe saluation consisteth faithe charitie thei abide haue woorkes dispraised reiected condemned neither thei suffer preache people wee muste onely looke saluation merites death workes christ therfore thei condemne accurse reuile blaspheme true christian doctrine wherein thei plainly discouer themselues vtterly blinde ignoraunt thei bee thynges whiche thei knowe owne naturall vnderstanding trentalles mass suche like legierdemaine whiche filleth bothe pouch paunch bryngeth store pelfe n wealth thereto thei whollie emploie themselues therby carie bothe themselues others perdition woe bee vnto haue followed waie cain cain killed brother none cause brother iuster godlier hymself god respect greater delight brother sacrifice therefore waie cain trust owne workes renounce reiecte workes bee true good workes deede finallie murther slaie walke truthe tight waie whiche nature practise wee see papistes earnestly tooth naile daiely put vre cast awaie deceit balaams wage thei bee inwardly hidden christ assured trust confidence god diuine grace thei licentiously breake actually dispose themselues sundrie sortes externall outward workes doe thinges greedinesse gaine pecuniarie reward fill beallies example prophete balaam declared seconde chapter second epistle peter aforegoyng perishe gainsaiyng core sedicious rebellion core wicked confederate swallowed earth wee reade fourth booke moses chapt xvj moses appoincted called god ende bryng conducte people israell egypt brother aaron bee high priest core beyng also tribe familie ambielously aspiryng cary high aucthoritie adioyned vnto hym twoo hundred fiftie captaines beste moste renoumed emong people raised vp suche mutinous faction seditious tumulte brought companie vprore welnere caused moses aaron flee giue place furie moses fallyng doune vppon face praied vnto lorde hee looke vnto offryng sacrifice spoken people thei separate themselues departe companie wicked conspiratours saied hereby ye shal knowe whether lord hath sent men dye common death men bee visited visitation men lorde hath sent lorde make newe thyng earth open mouthe swallowe downe men quicke pitte ye shall vnderstande men haue blasphemed prouoked lorde assoone made ende speakyng woordes euen grounde claue asunder thas vnder earth opened mouthe swallowed vp family men core goodes thei al thei went doune aliue pitte earth couered came fier fro lorde whiche consumed twoo hundred fiftie men adioyned themselues core offred incense example doeth sainct iude bryng horrible blasphemous popelynges charge v bee aucthours sedicion mutinie wee preache theim whereas deede thei causers garboile trouble christ aaron high priest onely ought heare acknowledge bishoppe soules pope greazed bishoppes abide thei aduaunce themselues alofte chalenge theim domination power flatly oppose themselues christe beeyng altogether drouned buried earthly conuersation pleasure beeyng verie worlde self doeth iude compare resemble core companion god straungely punished grounde opened swallowed vp aliue spottes feastes charitie whe thei feast without feare feedyng selues cloud thei without water caried windes corrupt tree without fruite twise dead plucked vp rootes thei ragyng waues sea fomyng owne shame thei wand yng staires reserued blackenesse darkenesse euer wee haue alreadie heard largelie discoursed epistle peter greater parte christendome hath trained brought vp child order priesthoode none cause liue idlie delicately without labour owne handes trouble preachyng voluptuouslie enioiyng spendyng owne ease pleasure goodes whiche poore men painfullie gotte sweate browes thei among common people reputed taken worthiest pillers iewelles ornamentes christian congregation whereas deede thei spotts wennes common wealth skumme filthe people detestable vizardes hypocriticall holinesse thei keepe iolie cheare fare moste deliciously accordyng old adage prouerbe whiche calleth delicate daintie cates morselles priest finallie thei without feare care verily thinkyng sathan hymself able ouerthrowe flocke thei feede nothyng rather themselues rauenous wolues deuoure eate vp sheepe thei cloudes caried high swaied alofte aire thei haue enstalled themselues chiefest place beste roumes carie credite countenance churche thei ought teache others thei care nothing al suffryng bee caried hither thither foggie miste errour ignoraunce deuill professed enemie mankinde thei also fruitlesse naked tree beginning winter bearing neither fruite leaues yet thei occupie roume tree doe thei beare shewe bishopps christ thei haue peece parte neither hym yet woordes workes dead rootes also ragyng waues sea euen windes sea tosse stirre waues waie waie thei also caried whither soeuer sathan driueth foame owne shame euen pot hath greate heate vnder thei full malice runneth ouer brim thei nozzeled spightfulnesse crueltie swellyng cankered stomackes holde must needes cast vp vomite beastly filthinesse therwith also defile pollute others wandryng starres call planetes retrograde hauyng motion backwarde like maner fellowes whose life doctrine nothyng errour seduce beguile bothe themselues followe therefore reserued mist darkenesse euer wordes example iude hath depaincted set massyng mate pollshorne prelate vnder name christ churche doe bring sea moste lewde execrable maners yet neuerthelesse vnder pretence thereof dooe catche rake vnto themselues wealth worlde bryng men heades vnder girdle enoch also seuenth adam prophecyed suche saiyng behold lorde commeth thousandes sainctes giue iudgment men place read scripture reason auncient father would admitt receiue epistle canonicall howbeit sufficient cause whereby disallowe reiect booke paule also ij timot iij nameth iannes iambres two aduersaries moses whose name notwithstandyng read whole byble beside howsoeuer men iudgements haue bee presently stande vpon poinct true god beginnyng worlde hath euer reueiled woorde wherein beleeuers grace saluation promised vnbeleeuers iudgement damnation threatened still continued euen till ascension christ whiche tyme word god hath openly generally preached ouer worlde natiuitie christ god still chose vsed certaine threede hande hande deliuer manifestation publication word first adam abraha dauid virgin marie mother christe others moe reueiled deliuered truth gospell therfore alwaies preached world neuer openly latter day sorte patriarch enoch preache publish word lorde whiche vndoubtedly learned father adam influence holy ghost recorded hym scripture gen v led vpright godly life therefore taken vp god seen wherevppon sprong fable hee come againe daye iudgement whiche thing bee looked vnlesse wee vnderstand sense shall come againe spirite namelie preachyng dooeth fitly iumpe agree tyme next afore generall iudgement present place truely agreeth thereto wherein speaketh certainly laste daie presently seene eye lorde saieth commeth thousandes sainctes infinite multitude word must needes vnderstood onely last daie wherein lorde come iudgement saintes first came worlde came many thousandes sainctes alone iudge giue grace rebuke vngodlie among wicked deedes whiche haue vngodlie committed place doth iude vnaptly inferre directly sounding false guide counterfaite teacher whiche knewe greate swarmes come little afore last daie seemeth also aptly beare interpretation signification lorde comming first destroye quight ouerthrowe pope al imperious potificalitie great mischieuous euill none helpe remedie vtter abolishyng quite takyng hym awaie long worlde endureth neither bee ende hym neither reformation amendment hym hoped truely place bee vnderstoode papistes miserably lamentablie seduce worlde forlorne desperate wicked life papistes possiblie imagined wherein thei impiously alreadie wallowe wil thei still continue worse worse pretending notwithstanding greate sanctimonie holinesse vnder name christe thei vse cloke contriue hide villaynous treacherie vnder name papistes wee may vnderstande rable seducyng imposter deceiuers beside shal come little last daie suche embrace follow godlesse impietie place therfore alle geth vnderstood last daie iudgement wee see speciallie meaneth saied iudgement looked whervpon wee conclude tyrannous shauelinges shauen tyrauntes tremblyng expectation reserued sorthe last daie commyng lorde whether come approche speede staie yet somewhat longer cruell speakynges whiche wicked synners haue spoken hym wordes reprooueth life reprehendeth saiynges much saie thei speake presumptuously malapertly lord commyng bee impudent tooto arrogant thei deryde blaspheme hym peter also epistle writeth speaketh life defiled deformed sinnes iniquity giuen ouer entierly addicted woorke impietie call impietie life led without faith although outwarde conuersation bee altogether flagitious damnable euill work deede fruictes impietie impietie self properly called life whiche glittereth outwardly gaie shew hypocriticall workes whereas harte vtterly voyde faithe suche impious person saieth lord reproue presumptuous doctrine whiche thei boldly teache thei stiflie defende obstinately maintaine leanyng alwaies owne brainsicke gloss construction sufferyng themselues bee conuerted turned truthe harder flint neuer desist condemnyng blasphemyng doctrine true godlinesse see liuely wordes enoch paint describe kinde person foyst themselues churche towarde latter ende worlde whiche vndoubtly ye papistes euery man euidently appeareth murmurer complainer walkyng owne lustes whose mouthes speake proude thynges man finde fault dealynges reproue vnlawful dissonaunt worde god shalbee sure bryng thereby pecke trouble murmure repine gnashe teeth example man leaue omit peece parte bishoppes ordinarie style wonted tytle straightwaies open throates crye contempt disobedience waie left withstand lawlesse lustes selfwilled dealinges thei bragge haue power bothe ouer body ouer soules thei haue gotten handes bothe swordes bee compelled lawe dooe iust right man preache thei hand abide haue exempted theselues maner taxe tribute imposition man dare touche thing belongeth vnto finallie thei growen degree tyrannie man dare presume preache worde contrarie order peeuish proceeding alledge scripture altogether bootelesse saie none maie expoud enterprete sauing thei themselues meanes come passe place thinges liue licentiously thei list saiynges bee wrested applied v professours true gospell wee reuerently dutifully submitt selues yeeld obedience aswell scripture ciuile power bothe whiche thei wilbe free compellable last al decree cannon pestered thwacked full proude arrogant swellyng wordes vtterly voyde good godlinesse hauing men persones admiration vantage hitteth nature disposition iumpe thei iudge thinges accordyng person whole pope canon ye shall finde commaunded bisshoppe humble beneath poore parishe priest fruictes christian life whatsoeuer al thinges rather sounde thus let curate bee vnder priest priest vnder bisshoppe bisshoppe vnder archbishoppe archbishoppe vnder patriarch patriarch vnder pope finallie euery one weare habite amyse weede cowle fashion clippe hayre shaue crowne beard make apparaile many benifices many prebendes might keepe c thus thei brought thinges certaine externall ceremony tradition makyng wholly occupied themselues mere childishe foolish friuolous trifle thei greate accoupt estimation yea thei iudged lesse deadly sinne man refuse adore reuerence boyishe toyes therefore well saieth iude place thei haue men person admiratio thei lappe vp lewd loude lye vizardes hypocrisie admire gaie shewes visiblie obiect eye thei neuer speake woorde neither knowe thyng knowe faith charitie crosse yet poore vulgare people suffer themselues still beesotted popishe bugges thinke themselues doe acceptable seruice god giuing good substaunce patrimonie feede filthie swine stye lewd sensualitie ye beloued remember woordes whiche spoken apostle lorde iesus christ thei told mocker laste tyme whiche walke owne vngodlie lustes place also giueth occasion thinke epistle written saincte iude apostle aucthour hereof reckeneth hymself among apostle speaketh theim though thei preached long tyme whereby maie well bee thought rather written godlie man read sainct peter epistle culled gathered woordes sentence mocker bee wee haue afore declared thei also bee walke owne lustes onely carnall fleshely lustes rather sauour horrible impietie wherin thei liue eche respect accordyng owne inordinate desire neither reuerencyng ciuile magistrate obeiyng worde god liue loosely contemptuously thei neither obediently acknowledge externall yet internal gouernement al lawes aswell diuine humaine thei flatly despise sette naught flye aire middle betweene heauen earth euen thei hoised vp caried aloft maister deuill maker sectes fleshely hauyng spirite alludeth whiche sainct peter epistle saied come false teacher whiche priuilie bryng damnable heresy thei disobediently breake asunder vnitie faithe beyng contented common profession generall appellation christian wherein eche one serue doe good neighbour thei deuise inuent certaine newe vpstart sectes owne wherby thei feigne false counterfaite seruice almightie god furthermore thei naturall fleshly brute beastes hauyng spirite vnderstandyng hath horse asse thei followe iudgement nature caried awaie concupiscence luste fleshe finallie thei haue worde god direct leade frame liues conuersations ye beloued edifie selues moste holie faithe praiyng holie ghoste keepe selues loue god fewe woordes hath briefly comprehended whole summe effect true christianitie faith grounde worke foundation wherevpon wee muste builde buildyng edifiyng daiely howrely profite goe foreward knowledge god lorde iesus christ whiche doen operation holie ghost beeyng sort builded wee dooe worke whereby purchase winne selues merite saluation onely profite doe good neighbour herein must wee haue moste diligent care wee continue perseuere true sincere loue without intermission dooe foolishe people whiche staie themselues vpon owne rotten workes deuise certaine peculiar sectes wherewith drawe awaie seduce men brotherly loue charitie lookyng forthe mercie lorde iesus christ vnto eternall life hope taught crosse commended life ought bee framed ledde bee nothyng el seruent sighyng longyng desire life come yet desire longyng muste bee whollie staied vppon onely mercie christe vnto wee muste ardently praie maie please hym euen owne mercie merite v take traslate v hence life come endlesse ioyes euer abounde haue copassion puttyng difference saue feare pullyng theim fier place somewhat darke obscure bee vnderstanded yet true meanyng thereof haue ye compassion saue leade liues maie euen greeue hart see miserablie blinded wilfully obstinate reioyce ye miserie neither take ye pleasure delite lamentable miscreauncie meddle ye atheisme separate selues theim haue dealyng companie ye maie pull greate daunger saue deliuer fearyng theim holding backe godlie seueritie deale courteously gentlie euen god hath dealt roughly ragyngly sharpely mieldely charitablie dooe churlishe sternesse terrifie spoile theim deale theim ye would lye fier ye ought carefull diligence wisely pul saue thei bee contented pulled deliuered thei gentle meanes tender mercie bee borne withall pope hereticall rabbines vse bee burned spoyled hate euen garment spotted fleshe haue receiued holie ghost faith thereby wee purified yet neuerthelesse long wee tie rotten sacke fleshe bloud still hangeth vpon v neuer without whose swarmes euill lustes spotted garment wee liue wee ought laie aside put vnto able keepe ye fal presente faultlesse presence glorie ioye god onely wise sauiour glorie maiestie dominion power bothe euer amen conclusion end epistle thus apostle wont ende writynges preachynges exhortation prophecy praie wishe giue thankes wee see therefore two epistle aswell iude seconde peter true christian life
